Gandhi's Declaration Before Departure 68

Presented Fourteen Demands to the British Governor

Denied the Acquired Rights of Foreigners

World News Agency reports that before embarking on this propaganda tour, Gandhi, the leader of the Indian Non-Cooperation Movement, published an article explaining his purpose and presenting fourteen demands to the British. The translation from the Indian newspapers is as follows:

"After many years of prayer and many years of sincere consideration of this issue, I have advised my compatriots to use non-cooperation to resist the British in our struggle for independence. But at the same time, I have tried to find a plan that would provide adequate provisions to avoid the recurrence of the Chaura incident, which would cause violent actions and disturbances. (Note: The Chaura Chauri incident referred to by Gandhi occurred in 1922 when Gandhi advocated the non-violent non-cooperation movement. Chauri Chauri is a village in the United Provinces of India. On February 1st of that year, a volunteer team of Gandhi's followers inspected a market and was blocked by police officers. On February 4th, the market reopened, and the volunteer team attacked the police station, setting it on fire. All personnel in the station, except for the workers, were killed, and their bodies were burned. A total of 24 policemen and militiamen were killed. After this incident, Gandhi fasted for five days to atone. He told people that he regarded this as God's warning that the non-cooperation movement was implemented too early, and it was his shame.)

Foreseeing that the time when India and Britain will meet in force may eventually come, India, standing against the wall, can hardly find an effective and harmless plan. In today's situation, it may not be possible to carry out the non-cooperation movement in the name of the Indian National Congress. It may be necessary to carry out individual non-cooperation movements without the formal participation of the Indian National Congress. Both are unknown, because everything in India today is still in its infancy. However, as it stands, it is harmful for the Indian National Congress to participate in the proposed meeting between Indian leaders and the British Governor. It can be asserted.

If the Indian National Congress wants to participate in this meeting, there must be at least one condition. This I dare to say is that the British government must declare in advance that this meeting will not discuss the Whippet plan, but will focus on a concrete plan to make India independent, and at the same time fulfill the conditions suitable for this meeting. If so, the leaders of the National Congress will be happy to respond.

This kind of meeting must have its cause, whether it comes from the goodwill of Britain, the pressure of world opinion, or the pressure from our side. We hope it comes from our pressure. If we can develop sufficient strength, we can achieve this result. The timing of its maturity depends entirely on our own efforts.

I further support the claim to deny certain Indian national debts. It should be known that the transfer of Indian rights to foreigners completely disregards the national interests of India. This is known to everyone. How can such national debts be expected, and how dare we ask an independent India to recognize them by invoking the cliché of so-called acquired rights?

British newspapers and our British rulers speak out and threaten that our non-cooperation movement and those who resist by force will suffer severe retribution. This is futile and useless. Although those who non-cooperate and those who resist by force have different methods, their goals are the same. Both have calculated the price and are willing to suffer pain, which cannot be suppressed by power.

Here, I record my plan, which can be called my fourteen points. Its content is the same as that presented to the Lords Lieutenant (former Governor-General of India). Now it is presented to the Earl of Irwin (current Governor-General of India), hoping that he and the British Cabinet will implement it voluntarily.

(1) Complete prohibition of alcohol, (2) the ratio of the rupee to the pound is reduced from one shilling and six pence to one shilling and four pence, (3)

The land tax is reduced by at least 50% and managed by the Legislative Assembly, (4) abolition of the salt tax, (5) military expenditure is reduced by at least half to reduce the tax rate accordingly, (7) protective tariffs are levied on imported foreign cloth, (8)

Passage of the Coastal Public Land Regulations, (9) release of political prisoners, except those who have committed murder or attempted murder, (10) withdrawal of all political accusations, (11) abolition of the sedition part of the criminal law, the 1918 regulations, etc., (12) permission for all deported Indians to return to India, (13) removal of the criminal inspection department, or public management of it, (14) issuance of licenses for firearms for self-defense, which are publicly managed,

The above are just the most urgent needs. In addition, there are

Page 12

should be reformed, which are too numerous to mention. Now, I would like to ask the Governor-General to satisfy India's simple and urgent needs. If the Governor-General can agree to these demands, the proposition of non-cooperation can be stopped, and the National Congress will be happy to participate in any meeting where it can express its views and make demands."

Local Notifications

Songjiang 69

False Alarm in Zhujing Last Night: Zhujing Town, Jinshan County, thirty-six miles from Songjiang, urgently called Songjiang last night (4th), requesting assistance. The troops recently deployed from Shanghai were asked to dispatch a team to provide assistance. The Public Security Bureau was instructed overnight to recruit guides to lead a company of troops to Zhujing to suppress the bandits. The First Team Headquarters of the Songjiang Water Public Security Bureau also reported the situation to the Minhang District Office and sent a team to suppress the bandits. Unexpectedly, the request for assistance from Zhujing was because several ships were seen sailing straight towards Zhujing. After ordering them to stop, it was learned that they were incense-burning boats returning from the Lianxuitang temple fair. After verification, the people of Zhujing were relieved. It is reported that the troops stationed in Songjiang, considering that Qingpu is also a place where lake bandits appear, also dispatched a company to Zhenshe

Recovery of Stolen Goods from the World English Hall and Arrest of the Main Criminal: After the ancient clock in the World English Hall in front of the old lifting department disappeared, County Magistrate Jin immediately ordered Inspector Yin to strictly investigate and arrest the culprits. It is now learned that a sand Ah Chang, who stole the clock, has been arrested and confessed to giving the stolen goods to Dai Tongxing. He has been transferred to the county government for questioning.

Zhangyan Town Has Not Yet Reopened: Since Zhangyan Town, Jinshan, was looted by bandits, the shops and residents have either lost all their property or their family members have been kidnapped. The sound of crying is unbearable to witness. To this day, the whole town is closed, and the scene is desolate. For example, Zhang, a physical education teacher at Liuxi Elementary School, had no family property and relied entirely on his meager salary to make a living. He was also kidnapped. His family only has an elderly mother. Losing this beloved son, she is in extreme pain. When the robbery occurred, the county magistrate received a telephone report but did not send police to rescue them. He also did not personally investigate the situation afterward, so the aftermath of the town has not yet been resolved. Extortion by bandits is also impersonated. Fengjing, which belongs to the county and is very close to Zhujing,

has been affected by Zhangyan in recent days, and rumors are rampant. The local regiment police are on high alert day and night. Small groups of local bandits in the villages near Fengjing, in groups of three or five, or more than ten people together, in addition to robbery, also extort money, almost every day. There are also those who lurk in sheds, rush out to intercept pedestrians, or strip them of their clothes. It is said that in the Bainiu Dang area north of Fengjing, people dare not walk alone even in broad daylight. It can be seen that bandits are everywhere, and thorns are all over the road. As for the act of extorting money, recently, in Linjiatang near the Land Temple, seven or eight bandits with iron rulers came a few days ago and extorted money from the families in the village who were slightly better off. Those who could not offer it on the spot were allowed to come and collect it on time, and some even wrote notes. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the third day, bandits came to collect the promised money, which was roughly from 30 to 200 or 300 yuan. Farmers carrying rice

to sell or scraping together their meager savings to meet the promised payment. However, not long after the bandits collected it, other bandits came to extort it, saying that they had just taken it away. They said that they were impostors and did not recognize it at all, causing endless disturbances. The villagers could not cope, so they smashed furniture and stoves to vent their anger and left disgruntled.

Qingpu 70

Lake Bandits Discovered at Guan Temple: At Guan Wang Temple near Zhujie Pavilion, the primary town in Qingpu County, over a hundred large and small bandit ships were discovered the day before yesterday. Fully equipped with firearms, they were extorting funds and seizing ships in nearby villages, spreading rumors of an impending raid on Zhujie Pavilion Town. Upon hearing the news, the town's water and land police forces immediately telegraphed the county government, requesting additional police units for joint suppression. Simultaneously, they dispatched teams to intercept the bandits. Upon receiving the report, the county government promptly sent a portion of the security regiment and telegraphed the Songhu Garrison Headquarters to request military assistance in the suppression. Yesterday, a company of infantry arrived from Shanghai to join forces with the police.

Shen Xiuwu Requests Divorce - A Court Hearing Record: Shen Xiuwu, a woman from this county, retained a lawyer to petition the county government, accusing her husband, Zhi Shangjiu, of abandonment and neglect, requesting a division of property and alimony of three thousand yuan for educational expenses. Yesterday, Judge Shen conducted a court hearing. Both the plaintiff and defendant were present. First, Shen Xiuwu was questioned. She stated that she was twenty-nine years old, a native of this county, and worked as a teacher. (Question) When did you marry Zhi Shangjiu? (Answer) September 25th of the fifteenth year of the Republic. (Question) Who was the matchmaker? (Answer) Initially, the defendant's family entrusted Chen Qizhou to make the introduction. Later, the defendant and I exchanged correspondence and formalized our relationship. The defendant personally proposed marriage multiple times before I agreed. Chen Qizhou served as the matchmaker for the engagement. (Question) Why did he abandon you? Does he not provide for you? (Answer) Since I married him, I have never been supported by him. I have always supported myself through education. Last October, he began to show signs of abandoning me. He stayed at a hotel during the New Year holiday and did not come home. Even when I encountered him on the road several times and tried to talk to him, he ignored me. Moreover, his mother did not allow me to stay at home and drove me out. The judge then questioned Zhi Shangjiu, who stated that he was twenty-seven years old, a native of this county, and worked as a teacher. (Question) The plaintiff said that you showed clear signs of abandoning her last October. (Answer) There was no act of abandoning her. (Question) Why didn't you go home during the New Year holiday last year? Why did you stay at a hotel? Did the plaintiff encounter you on the road and try to talk to you, but you ignored her? (Answer) Last year during the New Year holiday, I happened to bring the basketball team to Qingpu for a competition, so I stayed at a hotel. After the competition, I returned to school. The plaintiff's statement that she encountered me on the road and I ignored her is not true. (Question) Where did you stay during the winter vacation last year? (Answer) I stayed at home. She stayed at her parents' home and did not return. (Question) Why didn't you call her back since she didn't return? (Answer) Because on October 29th last year, the plaintiff and her father came to my school, insulted me, and cursed me.

That's why I didn't call her back. (Question) Now the plaintiff wants to separate from you, are you willing? (Answer) I am not willing. (Question) She is asking for three thousand yuan for educational expenses after the separation. (Answer) I have no money. At this point, the judge questioned Shen Xiuwu again. (Question) Now the defendant is unwilling for you to separate. You have been husband and wife for many years. Would it be better to remain together? (Answer) There have been many instances of his abandoning me, so I can only separate from him. The judge then instructed both parties to invite Chen Qizhou, Yang Lucun, and relatives to mediate. If an agreement cannot be reached within half a month, the case will be heard and judged again.

Suzhou 71

Citizens Petition Against Abolishing Suzhou Municipal Government: After the Suzhou Municipal Government was ordered to be abolished, Mayor Lu requested instructions from the provincial government. Chairman Ye instructed that the work should continue as usual, and the abolition should be temporarily suspended. However, recently, rumors have spread in Suzhou that the municipal government will be reorganized into a bureau, which does not seem to be the case. According to news from the municipal government, the provincial government intends to cut some redundant staff to save expenses. Now, citizens such as Xu Chuanzhu have petitioned the provincial government to withdraw the order to abolish the municipal government so that the only municipal government in Jiangsu can be preserved.

Li and Cheng Cross-Complaint Case Reopens for Debate: The case of defamation between Li Genyuan, a prominent figure in Suzhou, and his third concubine, Cheng Peiyi, was heard in the District Court on the 28th of last month. For Li's part of the accusation, the verdict was originally scheduled to be announced at 2:00 PM on the 31st. However, as of yesterday, the judgment had not been published. It is said that the court believes that this case still requires continued debate, so a second debate will be scheduled before the verdict is announced.

Deadline of Ten Days to Construct Two County Roads: The Wuxian County Construction Bureau is actively carrying out the requisition of labor for the construction of various county roads. Funding for the Wujin and Nantong county courts will also be increased starting in April, and salaries for prison staff will be increased by 2,500 yuan per month.

Wuxi 72

Zhenxin Cotton Mill to Resume Operations Soon: The Zhenxin Cotton Mill outside Ximen has been closed for several years. Although shareholders have repeatedly prepared to resume operations, various difficulties have prevented it from happening. Recently, preparations have been completed, and all difficulties have been resolved. Operations are scheduled to resume soon.

Armed Clash at Luoshe Xiangfan: During the Xiangfan festival in Luoshe Town, Wan'an City, 16th District, villagers from various villages pooled funds to put on operas to honor the gods. This year, it was held as usual and was quite lively. However, around 7:00 PM yesterday, Zhou Xianglin from Fengzhuang had a quarrel with a certain Jia from Duanjiaqiao over a trivial matter, which led to a fight. Zhou was outnumbered and injured all over his body. He immediately fled back and gathered many people, each holding broadswords and iron weapons, to seek revenge. The two sides engaged in an armed clash on the open space next to the Luoshe Weicheng Silk Factory. As a result, Xu Acai and Jiang Jinrong from Duanjiaqiao were wounded in the head by broadswords wielded by people from Fengzhuang. The Luoshe Chamber of Commerce arrested two accomplices from Fengzhuang and presented them to the county government for investigation along with the injured from both sides yesterday.

Petition to Change Regulations for Wood Transportation and Distribution: Various types of timber sold by the Wuxi Timber Industry are imported from Liyang Nandao and Shanghai, with full taxes paid at the first tax checkpoint. Tax receipts are held, and the timber is transported to Wuxi for retail distribution to various villages. In the past, there were no inspections or additional taxes at the tax checkpoints. However, since the establishment of a special bureau for timber tax, the regulations have suddenly changed. Now, the timber industry must exchange import tax receipts for distribution permits, which are valid for three months. If the deadline is exceeded, additional taxes must be paid. In the past month, disputes have frequently arisen between the special tax bureau and various firms in the industry, with endless arguments. The industry convened a general meeting and unanimously agreed that since the county has no timber products of its own, they must be transported from other provinces. The timber is bulky and slow-moving, and imports cannot be easily evaded like other goods. It takes a long time to sell, often a year and a half to clear the stock. Since the implementation of the new regulations, it has not only been difficult to operate but also the tax checkpoints often take the opportunity to create difficulties and extort money. It is requested that the new regulations be changed as soon as possible to comply with the principle of "one tax per item." Yesterday, the industry submitted a petition to the County Chamber of Commerce to forward it to the authorities, hoping to achieve the goal of revocation. The Chamber of Commerce forwarded a letter to the General Branch of the Special Tax Bureau, requesting that the new regulations be changed as soon as possible to alleviate the difficulties of businesses.

Closing Waterways Between Kunshan and Wuxi: The Jinghu Railway, from Kunshan to Wuxi, has many rivers and complex waterways, making it difficult to monitor the boats coming and going. Recently, due to rampant lake bandits, bandit ships have been hiding everywhere, making it difficult for the military and police to search. The Taihu Bandit Suppression Headquarters convened a meeting of bandit suppression in the counties around the lake on the 31st of last month and resolved to close all waterways between Wuxi and Kunshan. Yesterday, General Commander Hu instructed the county chiefs of Wuxi, Wuxian, and Kunshan, as well as the district chiefs of the Second and Third Water Police Districts and the public security bureaus of the three counties, to comply with the resolution of Article 5 of the bandit suppression plan. All waterways that do not impede traffic must be closed by the 20th of this month. All ships coming and going must be inspected. The district chiefs of the Second and Third Water Police Districts were ordered to dispatch teams to strictly guard the key points of the waterways to facilitate the suppression.

Another False Alarm at Xueyanqiao: Xueyanqiao Town, at the junction of Changzhou and Wuxi, has become a flock of startled birds since it was looted by lake bandits last year. The day before yesterday, more than twenty out-of-towners suddenly arrived in the town, acting suspiciously. The town feared that it would repeat the disaster of last year and was panicked. Yesterday, a special commissioner was sent to Wuxi to report to the Second Water Police District, requesting that a team be dispatched for protection. Upon receiving the report, District Chief Mao immediately took the Jialu patrol ship to the town to reassure the people and dispatched Han Yunbo's unit from the 10th Company of Changzhou to take appropriate precautions to avoid any mistakes.

Department Appoints Investigator for County Government Land Sale Case: The Wuyi County Government, under two county magistrates, Zhang and Zhu, requested to move the old county government office to the county middle school, while the county middle school would be rebuilt elsewhere. It was planned to sell the original county government site, and someone reported this to the Department of Civil Affairs and the Department of Construction. Huang investigated at the county party headquarters and the county chamber of commerce and decided to return to the province on the 5th to report.

County Government Convenes Meeting to Maintain Food Supply: The Wuyi County Government, due to high rice prices, which have risen to 16 or 17 yuan per stone, convened a meeting of officials and gentry on the afternoon of the 4th to maintain the food supply. After detailed discussion, it was decided that the chamber of commerce and the district offices would investigate the rice merchants inside and outside the city, the recent amount of inventory, and whether there was any hoarding or speculation. After the investigation, another meeting will be held to discuss purchasing rice and selling it at a fair price.

Express Boat Robbed on Xiaohai River: An express boat from Xiaohai Town, Wuyi County, to Beniu was robbed by three thieves who boarded the boat near Huangniba, Shuitaikou, the night before last. All goods, silver, and clothing were robbed.

Nantong 74

First Execution in Dongxiang: Bandits and communists were rampant in Dongxiang, Nantong. After joint suppression by the navy, army, police, and security forces, the main force of bandits and communists retreated to Caopeng Town. Their false commander-in-chief, Jiang Laowu, was captured in Beishan Port on the 3rd. After interrogation by the police headquarters on the 4th, he was executed at Erjia Town at noon. His head was hung in the area where the incident occurred as a warning.

Two Police Captains Removed from Office: The Nantong County Police Team lost 77 rifles, many bullets, Mauser pistols, and handguns to bandits in Dongxiang. After discussions by various sectors, it was decided that the team captain, Yan Diannan, should be responsible for recovering the lost weapons and ammunition. On the day of the incident, Company Commander Xu Guanxiong was in Erjia Town

Patronizing prostitutes and having fun. Squad Leader Wu Xuxi fled without fighting. Xu and Wu should both be removed and punished. On the 4th, the county government ordered the county police headquarters to send Xu and Wu to the county for further instructions from the provincial government.

Lusi Sea Bandits Repelled: Guan Shou, a follower of the deceased sea bandit Pan Kaiqu, led a group of 300 bandits to occupy Lusi Sanjia Town. One group of about 80 people, carrying Mauser pistols, arrived at Lusi Town in small carts and looted extensively. Later, the bandit leader Shen Guanshou died of illness in Sanjia Town. The bandits held a memorial service on the 2nd. The Songhu Battalion Commander Liu led a team to suppress them and used machine guns to strafe them, killing more than 70 bandits. The rest fled to the sea. Lusi is now peaceful.

Gong Qian Sent to County for Legal Action: Gong Qian, the chief of the urban public security bureau, enticed two young women, Zhou and Yang, to go sightseeing and held a gambling party at He's residence. After the event, the two girls suddenly disappeared. After being reported, the county bureau dismissed Gong and sent him to the county government. County Chief Chen requested instructions on how to handle Gong, as he was appointed by the Department of Civil Affairs. Zhou Junchi, the father of Zhou, has filed a complaint with the county against Gong and requested that his daughter be returned.

Provincial Government Closes Beijing Office: After the Jiangsu Provincial Government moved from Beijing to Zhenjiang, it established an office in Beijing to facilitate operations and kept a guard team stationed in Beijing. Now, the provincial government is striving to streamline all its affiliated institutions, so it plans to abolish this institution to save money. Were led to Zhenjiang by Captain Shen and First Squad Leader Lin Bin.

Hotel Tax Implemented: The Zhenjiang County Education Bureau previously requested the authorities to collect a hotel tax to fund public education. However, the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce and the Hotel Industry Branch refused to recognize it, so it was temporarily suspended. Later, the need for education funds became urgent. The county government submitted a report on the handling situation to the Department of Finance, which forwarded it to the provincial government. Now, the provincial government has issued an instruction that the donation should be approved and collected as it is specifically for public education purposes. It should be specially stored and used and should not be arbitrarily allocated, otherwise, the original plan will be violated.

Yangzhou 76

Dispute Over Fineness of Silver Refining: Yesterday, several former workers from the Baosheng and Baoqing silver shops, which have already closed, went to the two silver shops and purchased twelve silver pendants from children's hats, obtained invoices, and brought them to the Public Security Bureau, claiming that the silver pendants were of very poor quality and that the two silver shops were selling them as full-fineness silver, deceiving customers. They requested that officials be dispatched immediately for on-site testing. Director Zhao then assigned two inspectors to take testing equipment and go to the two silver shops for separate testing. The results showed that they only contained 70% silver. The Public Security Bureau considered the accusation to be true and arrested Wu Huirun, Zhang Xicheng, and Fu An, employees of the silver shops, intending to send them to the county for legal action. Later, a standing committee member of the Chamber of Commerce came forward to bail them out and mediated the matter.

Execution of Four Convicted Robbers and Murderers: On February 5th, the home of Li Buyun, a resident of Xiaochen Village, Wayaopu, in the county, was robbed and burned, and Li Busheng was burned to death. The Jiangtai Public Security Team, the Water Public Security Team, and the Police Team successively arrested Yu Qingfa, Wang Xiaominzi, Zhang Da'aizi, Geng Sizi, etc.

They were sent to the Jiangdu County Government. The suspects confessed to the robbery, assault, murder, and distribution of spoils. Now, the county has presented the case to the provincial government and the death penalty has been approved. Today (the 4th) at 2:00 PM, the four convicts were taken to the execution ground behind Erlang Temple for execution by firing squad.

Jiangyin 77

Hua Cheng Cloth Factory Labor Dispute Calmed: The female workers in the iron machine department of the Hua Cheng Cloth Factory went on strike over wage issues. On the 3rd, Zhong Jianhui, the director of training of the County Rectification Committee, mediated the dispute and negotiated with Wu Shuying, the manager of the factory, and others, and the following regulations were set: (1) The price of each foot of iron machine cloth will be increased by five yuan, and the price of each plate head will be increased by ten yuan. The price of each board of yarn will be increased by five yuan, and the price of each disc will be increased by ten yuan. (2) Bonuses and penalties will be implemented for at least ten months each year, with an additional five yuan added to the price as before and a reduction of two-thirds of the fine as before. (3) The shed door will be open from 10:00 AM to 1:00 PM every day. (4) Wages will be paid for legal holidays stipulated by the central government. (5) Female workers may not be dismissed without cause. (6) In case of labor disputes, the legal procedures should be followed, and work should not be stopped without cause. The above cases should be strictly observed by both parties and will be implemented from April 4th.

News of the Zhou Case Verdict: Zhou Shuiping was questioned and completed in the Wu County District Court on the 26th of last month, and the verdict was scheduled to be announced. According to news from Suzhou, the case was judged on the 1st, and Wang Tingyi, Li Chengmin, and Wang Wenru were all declared innocent. Whether this is true remains to be verified.

Xue Shibao Feels His Fate in Prison: The case of Xue Shibao of Tangtouqiao, Sihe Township, brutally killing Chen Ruilin and others, the county government originally scheduled to summon Xue Peiying and others to court for questioning on the 7th. Now Huang Youbo and others plan to ask the county to postpone the court session to the 11th. Xue Shibao is in prison, feeling his fate, and wrote another poem. The original sentence is: "A generous determination to eliminate enemies has not been achieved, half a lifetime of career has been overturned in one morning, fame has misled me into a strange robbery, creation deceives people and makes things uneven, there is no stomach for a bloody petition, the heart accompanies the prison with glory, (eldest daughter Pei Xiu Yue'er), the prison drips with cool tears, the firewood and gall anticipate the hope of future generations," such as

Petition to Severely Punish County Chief Liu: County Chief Liu Changyan of Ru county is greedy, cruel, cunning, and has committed many evils. He was ordered by the provincial government to be removed from office and investigated. Now, travelers in Shanghai trace his various crimes of recklessly killing, recklessly burning, recklessly detaining, and recklessly arresting, deceiving the superiors and wronging the people. Not only should he be punished administratively, but he also has serious crimes under criminal law. If he is allowed to remain at large, the administration will never be clear and the banditry will never be eliminated. Therefore, we specifically petition the provincial government to arrest Liu and hand him over to the judiciary for severe punishment to restore the decaying atmosphere.

Nantong Bandit Forces Have Been Defeated: On the night of the 28th of last month, a bandit force in Nantong attempted to flee west from Shigang but was intercepted by the defense forces. They fled east again. In the south of Caobu, Matang District of this county, they came into contact with the provincial police. The security forces of the Matang and Jue districts heard the news and went to rescue them, killing more than 40 bandits. At the moment, the Juegang security forces are focusing all their efforts on the coastal defense. The provincial police and the Matang security forces are stationed in Caobu. Yesterday (30th) more than a hundred provincial police officers arrived, and the security of Dongxiang can be guaranteed.

Laohuzhuang Was Attacked and Repelled: At about 12:00 on the night of the 30th, many bandits launched an attack on Laohuzhuang in Motou. The 9th squad of county police stationed in the village opened fire and returned fire for a while, and the bandits were unable to withstand it and retreated.

Gaoyou 78

Chajiadian Robbery Case: Cha Peilan, a farmer in Chajiadian, in the county, purchased more than 20 mu of paddy fields from the Chen family in Taoduo Village this spring, priced at more than 1,000 yuan, scheduled to pay on the day before yesterday. On the 1st of this month, at the second watch of the night, seven or eight robbers suddenly came, speaking in the local dialect. Each held a gun and broke into the door, tied up Cha Yun, and burned Cha's breasts with fire. Cha, in unbearable pain, then said that the price of the field had been paid to the Chen family, so the bandits went to Taoduo Village to rob the Chen family, and the losses were quite large. The Guo and Wang families in Yigou Township were also robbed by bandits that night, with losses of about three or four hundred yuan.

Hangzhou 79

Establishment of Maritime Affairs Bank: The Zhejiang Provincial Maritime Affairs Bureau plans to establish a Maritime Affairs Bank to regulate the maritime economy and promote its development. The minimum capital must be more than 500,000 yuan. Yang Peiwen, the chief of the accounting section of the bureau, is currently planning everything. Once the budget is set, it will be submitted to the provincial government meeting for discussion.

National Products Mobile Exhibition: The Hangzhou National Products Mobile Exhibition will be held today

Opening ceremony. More than 80 national product manufacturers from Shanghai and Hangzhou participated. The Provincial Party Department was elected as the presidium of the conference. The order of the meeting is as follows: (1) Opening of the meeting, (2) Playing music, (3) Singing the party song, (4) Giving the most respectful salute to the party, national flag, and the portrait of the Premier, (5) Reading the will respectfully, (6) Silence, (7) Chairman reports the purpose of the meeting, (8) Preparatory committee reports preparations, (9) Speech, (10) Playing music, (11) Photography.

Xiaoshan 80

Price Disclosure of Fourth Township Silkworm Cocoons: The East and West Townships in Xiaoshan have traditionally been engaged in silkworm rearing. It is learned that the sand farmers of the two townships convened a meeting on the 1st to disclose the current price. It is reported that the East Township agreed on the spot to disclose the price of eight yuan per 100 catties of silver dollars, and the West Township disclosed the price of nine yuan and two jiao per dan. However, the area around Xixing is only worth five or six yuan due to the harm caused by sand and mud on the car roads.

Severely Punish Corrupt Tax Collectors: The tax collectors, Chen Yun, etc., stationed in the Anchang Flower Tax Bureau in Changhe Town, Xiaoshan, exceeded their authority and imposed arbitrary fines. After investigation by the Finance Department Committee, it was found to be true, and they were sent to the court for legal action to recover the fine. The original bureau chief was recorded for dereliction of duty as a warning. The plan to reorganize the Qiantang River water conservancy. The Zhejiang Provincial Water Conservancy Bureau, in order to facilitate the water transportation of the inner rivers and outer seas of Zhejiang Province, had a plan to connect the Qiantang River with the Grand Canal. However, the bureau believes that in order to connect the Qiantang River with the Grand Canal, the Qiantang River must be reorganized first. Now, the river channel is silted up near the gate, which is almost level with the water surface, making it difficult for ferries and transportation, and the time and cost are both lost. Its inconvenience to travelers and merchants can be imagined. Since Hangzhou is the provincial capital, and the Qiantang River is an important route for traffic to and from the east and west of Zhejiang, the reorganization of the Qiantang River should not be delayed for a moment.

Reassignment of a Large Number of Public Security Bureau Chiefs: Wang Zhijue, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs, reassigned the public security bureau chiefs of eight counties yesterday: Zhang Shizhong of Hao County, Wu Zikai of Huoqiu, Ma Dong of Fuyang, Feng Zuguang of Fanchang, Liu Wenqi of Taihe, Hong Ximou of Luan, Zhang Weizhi of Qimen, and Ke Changqi of Huaiyuan.

The Initial Results of Naval Student Recruitment in Anhui Are Announced: The Department of Education held the preliminary examination for naval students on the 1st, and five students including Pan Duo Jin, Yang Guang Yao, Fang Ben Shan, Zuo Ke Xi, Qian Bang Yan, etc. have been admitted. These students should report to the Navy Department for examination before April 10th.

Hefei 82

Bandit Situation in He, Lu'an, Shu, and Lu Counties: Bandits and communists in the western townships of Lu'an, Mapu, and Dushan have just retreated, and bandit forces in the eastern townships of Jinqiao, Guanting, and Chunshugang are on the rise again. Dozens of freight trucks transporting goods from Fei to Lu'an were robbed on the way. Starting from the 30th, businesses in Lu'an have been calling one after another to stop transporting goods to avoid losses. More than a thousand bandits of the Quan Guangyi force entrenched in the Sanjuesi area at the junction of He and Shou counties suddenly left on their own and fled into the Zhuangmuqiao, Zhangbaling, and Baliwan areas in Shu County, extensively burning and looting, shocking Shucheng. County Chief Li Guokai of Shu personally led the security battalion to suppress the bandits and was repelled. The bandits in Sanhe Town at the junction of He, Lu, and Shu counties have risen again. County Chief Li is now in Sanhe and has decided to hold a joint defense meeting of the three counties of He, Lu, and Shu. Lujiang County has sent Commissioner Wang to participate. The Sanhe Chamber of Commerce has requested County Chief Wang of Hefei to go on April 1st to participate in the council to facilitate the suppression. However, the bandit atmosphere in Sanwenhe, Shikou, and Changlinhe in the eastern townships of Hefei is also fierce. County Chief Wang sent Huang Luzhen, the leader of a self-defense regiment, to lead a team to raid the villages this afternoon (30th).

Murder Case Arising from Marital Discord: Gong, the wife of Shi Danie and Shi Guizhi of Gaoqiao, Beifuguo, has had illicit relationships with her relatives, Guihai and Guiying. The night before (27th), Guihai and Gong were having fun when Guiying found out. Burning with jealousy, he went with a knife, broke into the door, dragged Guihai out, and hacked him to death with dozens of knives. The Shi family was alarmed and captured Guiying and Gong and sent them to the county for punishment.

Chu Minyi Set Sail Yesterday 83

▲Attending the Belgian Exposition

Central Committee Member Chu Minyi set sail on the French mail ship Athos yesterday afternoon to Europe, representing our country to attend the centennial commemorative exhibition of the founding of Belgium. He is scheduled to stay in Europe for half a year before returning to China. Many people from all walks of life saw him off. The Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce prepared a small steamboat with colorful decorations to carry Chu and those who came to see him off from the Xinguang Wharf to Songkou. Fireworks were set off along the way. Those who came to see him off included Li Shizeng, Wang Xiaolai, Yuan Ludeng, Lin Kanghou, and the French Consul and dozens of others. Chu's relatives and friends gave many flower baskets. As Chu boarded the ship and set off, he waved the national flag on the deck.

The Rice Market Has Eased 84

▲Few Rice Shipments

▲Prices of all rice have fallen slightly

Yesterday, the Social Affairs Bureau still sent cadres to investigate the situation in the rice market in the north and south city rivers. In the south city, the prices of old Songjiang rice, rice from Chefang, Qingpu, and Langxia have all fallen by three or four jiao. However, since the Social Affairs Bureau set a price limit on rice from Tongli, the number of ships arriving has decreased sharply. Even if one or two ships arrive, the price is still required to be 18 yuan. Although the price of rice can be lowered, the deliberate holding up of rice from Tongli has some slight impact. Also yesterday afternoon, Fu Changbang, a dealer from the Social Affairs Bureau, Zhang Chengxian, came to the bureau for questioning, reportedly about the matter of six or seven ships of Changbang rice being held up for sale. After investigation, the Social Affairs Bureau ordered that the price limit should not be used as the standard. The market has declined, and prices should be reduced according to the market. In the north city, southern rice is still priced at 18 yuan, and there are still no buyers. The highest quality white japonica rice is 19 yuan and two jiao, and only a few transactions have been made. The market has eased, and the future market is still expected to decline. On the production side, seeing that the Shanghai market is sluggish, prices are also falling step by step, falling more than one yuan compared to the highest price.

Shigemitsu Discusses Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement 86

▲ Negotiation to Begin in Beijing on Tuesday

▲ Sino-Japanese Press Circle Hosted at a Banquet Yesterday

Regarding the Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement, Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting and Japanese Minister Shigemitsu Aoi have already signed a draft agreement in Beijing. Yesterday, Mr. Shigemitsu told our reporter that the agreement is currently under review by the Privy Council of the Japanese government and is expected to be approved in about a week. When he receives instructions, he will go to Beijing to formally sign the agreement with Minister Wang.

▲ Negotiations on Extraterritoriality

Reports say that Shigemitsu Aoi was scheduled to meet with Wang Zhengting in Shanghai yesterday to negotiate the abolition of extraterritoriality. When the reporter asked Shigemitsu about this, he replied that he had other appointments in the past few days, so he did not have time to meet with Minister Wang today. However, he has decided to go to Beijing next Tuesday to discuss public and private matters with Mr. Wang. Since Minister Wang will still be in Shanghai on Monday, he may pay him a visit. He believes that the tariff issue is the most difficult in Sino-Japanese treaty negotiations. Now that the difficult hurdle has been overcome, the remaining issues, such as extraterritoriality, can be expected to be resolved gradually if both sides are willing to negotiate.

▲ Banquet for Sino-Japanese Press Circle

Yesterday afternoon, Minister Shigemitsu Aoi hosted a banquet for the Sino-Japanese press circle at the Japanese Club. On the host's side, Chargé d'Affaires Shigemitsu, Secretary Hayashi, Secretary Horiuchi, Secretary Morio, Consul Miura, Consul Okazaki, Consul Iguchi, Consul Tanaka, and Mr. Kan Seimatsu attended. On the guest side, reporters from Shen Bao, Xinwen Bao, Jiji Xinbao, Guomin Xinwenshe, and Zhonghua Dianxunshe attended. Representatives from Shibao and Minguo Ribao were absent. Reporters from Shanghai Nichi Nichi Shimbun, Shanghai Mainichi Shimbun, Shanghai Jiji Shimbun, Osaka Asahi Shimbun, Osaka Mainichi Shimbun, Osaka Jiji Shimpo, Jiangnan Wanbao, Japan United News Agency, and Japan Telegraphic Communication Agency also attended. Chairman Shigemitsu delivered a welcome speech, hoping for mutual understanding between the two sides, and introduced the embassy secretaries and the consuls of the Shanghai Consulate General. Finally, Pan Gongbi gave a reply on behalf of the press circle.

French Municipal Council 92

Motions of the Health Committee Meeting

▲ Mass Vaccination Against Cholera and Smallpox

The Health Committee of the French Concession of this city held a meeting at 5:00 PM on March 21st of this year in the council chamber of the Municipal Council. Mr. Li Rong was elected as chairman. Attendees included committee members Baron and Gubier, Superintendent of the Municipal Council Wei Zhiren, Director-General Truelle, Director of the Health Bureau, Doctor of Medicine Anhe, and Chief of the Health Department, Bogaert. Based on the recommendation of the former Ministry of Health of the Chinese National Government, a Cholera Prevention Health Committee meeting was convened in this city on March 1st of this year. Representatives from the Municipal Government of this city and the two concession Public Works Departments attended and participated. The purpose of the meeting was to guide the residents of Shanghai to understand the methods of preventing the spread of cholera. At the meeting, the report of Dr. Stommens, Chairman of the International Quarantine Committee, was read first. The representatives from the Shanghai Special Municipal Government and the two concession Public Works Departments discussed the various proposals to be adopted from May 1st. As a result, they were generally approved. The proposals are as follows: (1) Post advertisements, distribute leaflets, and, to the extent possible, produce films to show the audience, so that they all know the general principles of hygiene. (2) Provide free vaccination against smallpox to prevent residents from being infected with cholera, which is especially important in densely populated and easily infected areas. The Health Committee of this concession believes that the various policies agreed upon by the three municipal authorities contain the nature of gradually educating the public. In the opinion of the three municipal administrative authorities, establishing a printed advertising agency to carry out thorough publicity so that residents know the methods of preventing cholera would be even more effective. The anti-epidemic propaganda films distributed and screened by the Shanghai Special Municipal Government should be vigorously promoted. The French Municipal Council is willing to sacrifice a large sum of money each year for the cleaning and hygiene of this concession, and cannot be stingy in resisting this particularly dangerous cholera epidemic. Therefore, the Committee proposes to add an item of expenditure to the unexpected expenditure column of the Municipal Council's budget table for the establishment of an epidemic prevention medical office on May 1st. The medical office plans to employ three doctors, two nurses, and three assistants to form three shifts to take turns inoculating cholera vaccines. The above-mentioned mobile medical office will circulate within the concession area during the specified period, so that the residents of this concession can easily receive free vaccination against cholera. In winter, the medical office can also inoculate vaccines against smallpox and measles. These preventive measures will be very effective, so it is hoped that residents will understand the intention of the Municipal Council and ensure that this public welfare undertaking does not go to waste. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM. Subsequently, the Municipal Council meeting of the French Municipal Council approved the cholera vaccination measures proposed by the above-mentioned Health Committee meeting. The Board of Directors also resolved to open another expenditure item in the unexpected expenditure column of the budget table for the organization of the vaccination office, materials, and equipment.

Second Joint Meeting on Overseas Chinese Postal Rate Increase 93

The Overseas Chinese Federation, the National Federation of Commerce, the Overseas Chinese Affairs Advancement Association, Jinan University, the Nanyang Culture Department, the Nanyang Students Association, and other organizations, in order to fight for the overseas Chinese postal rate increase case, organized a joint meeting and elected Chen Zhiying, Xu Jigong, Chen Chunan, Zheng Qizhong, Lin Jingxian, Zhu Xiajiu, Shan Wuchu, and other seven people as general representatives to prepare for all matters related to the case. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the general representatives held a second meeting. Situ Shangshen, Standing Committee member of the Overseas Chinese Federation, also attended and participated. A letter was sent in advance inviting Lin Bao, Director-General of the Postal Administration, to attend and participate. The Postal Administration was unable to attend and dispatched Yu Xianglin, Director of the General Affairs Department, and Xu Yingzhi, a member of the committee, to explain the situation of the case and report that the Ministry of Communications had sent a winter telegram stating that the postage for domestic overseas Chinese mail sent to Nanyang had been reduced to five cents per twenty grams, and that the British Postal Bureau in Nanyang had been contacted to discuss the matter. They also reported on the progress of establishing special postal agency offices. The general representatives stated that the five cents for domestic mail sent to Nanyang and the six cents for foreign mail sent back to China were requested by the Overseas Chinese Congress in Singapore and there would be no objection. However, they requested that the official letter from the Postal Administration be sent to the meeting so that it could be forwarded to organizations in Singapore and Shantou and Xiamen. Director Yu agreed to do so, and the meeting was adjourned. The Overseas Chinese Federation immediately telegraphed Singapore to report the progress of the postage reduction.

Foreign Shipping Companies Refuse Pilot Wage Demands 94

▲ Chinese Ships Have Resumed Service

Taegu, Yili, Nisshin, and Jiangjiang and other foreign steamship companies have collectively suspended navigation due to the upstream Yangtze River pilots demanding a wage increase. This disrupted the traffic on the Sichuan River. They also intend to cause economic pressure and panic among the pilots, leading them to voluntarily abandon their wage increase requests. At the same time, they also issued a notice to our Chinese merchants to join in solidarity, so that they could monopolize the upstream navigation rights. Now that the Chinese merchants have seen through their intentions and refused to be exploited, they have resumed their businesses. The details of this matter are as follows:

▲ Pilot Wage Increase Demands

Among our country's various pilots, only the Sichuan River uses all Chinese pilots. Those employed by foreign merchant ships such as Taegu, Yili, Nisshin, and Jiangjiang, receive unequal treatment in terms of wages compared to Chinese ships. Moreover, their promotions are suppressed. The pilots have suffered deeply from this mistreatment, and at the end of last month, they proposed wage increase demands. Second-class pilots requested a 50% increase, and third-class pilots requested a 40% increase, with gradual annual increases. The wage for first-class pilots should be increased to $500, second-class pilots to $400, and third-class pilots to $200. Furthermore, first-class, second-class, and third-class pilots should each receive a monthly food allowance of $50, $40, and $30. Taegu and Nisshin and others strongly opposed accepting these demands and suspended all upstream ships, indicating that there was no room for compromise. As a result, traffic on the Sichuan River was disrupted.

▲ All Chinese Ships Resume Service

After the pilots put forward their demands, they clarified to the Chinese shipping companies that their actions were purely aimed at external demands and seeking a guarantee for their livelihood. When the foreign ships collectively suspended navigation, they ordered the 11 Chinese shipping companies operating upstream to suspend their services as well. The Chinese merchants refused to sign the agreement, and the British and Japanese merchants immediately accused them of disrupting the industry and negotiated with the Shanghai headquarters of each company. The companies politely declined and, starting on the 1st of this month, companies such as Sanbei and Yujiang, in order to maintain the commercial traffic between Sichuan, Hankou, and Shanghai, agreed to add a food allowance of $30 per person to the pilots and continue to work as usual. Starting from the 3rd, six Chinese ships, including Wuxing, Yujiang, Jiujiang, Hejiang, Wan'an, and Dingyuan, have resumed their service, and traffic between Sichuan and Shanghai has been restored. Goods from Shanghai to Sichuan can now be loaded and shipped.

▲ Jiangjiang Ships Also Resume Service

When the Chinese ships began to operate, foreign officials at the Yichang Customs Office spoke on behalf of the British and Japanese shipping companies and prohibited the Chinese ships from carrying goods. This was stopped after protests from the Chinese merchants. The American merchant Jiangjiang Company, which has six ships operating upstream, also acknowledged the pilots' demands independently and increased the salaries of each person by $30 according to their rank and provided a food allowance of $30. Therefore, they also resumed their service as usual from the previous day. However, Taegu, Yili, and Nisshin and other three companies still firmly refuse to increase wages and would rather suffer the sacrifice of suspending operations than accept the demands. It is known that these three companies have a total of 18 ships suspended.

▲ Soldiers Dispatched to Ships for Escort

In recent times, bandits have been rising upstream of Yichang, intercepting and looting merchant ships. This has been a frequent occurrence. In order to protect the safety of the Chinese ships that have resumed their service, in addition to installing bulletproof steel plates, they have publicly requested Guo Rudong's 20th Army to dispatch 12 armed soldiers per ship to provide escort and prevent attacks by bandits.

▲ Business Declines and Prices Reduced

Recently, although foreign ships have suspended operations and the number of ships has decreased, many merchants in Sichuan dare not ship goods due to the chaotic situation, resulting in a shortage of both upstream and downstream goods. Among the goods shipped to Sichuan, cotton yarn is the most common. Recently, various shipping companies have planned to further reduce the freight rate for yarn from $8 per piece to $6 per piece. This is currently being discussed and will be implemented soon.

Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities 97

Suggestions for Rectifying City Telephone Services

▲ Ten Points Listed

▲ Consultation with the Ministry for Adoption

The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities considers telephones as one of the most important municipal facilities, closely related to the development of municipal industries, the maintenance of municipal public safety, the advancement of municipal transportation, and the progress of all other municipal affairs. It has been found that there are many aspects of the city's telephone system that need rectification. Although there have been plans, they could not be implemented before the jurisdictional issues of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau were resolved. However, for the benefit of the citizens, the Bureau cannot ignore the situation. Therefore, it has formulated opinions on several major areas that are considered urgently in need of rectification and submitted them to the Municipal Government for consultation with the Ministry of Communications. The Ministry is requested to instruct the Shanghai Telephone Bureau to implement these measures effectively to benefit the municipality. The rectification opinions are as follows:

(1) Amend the business regulations. The Shanghai Telephone Bureau stipulates that the business scope of the Nanshi area extends north to the French Concession, east and south to the Huangpu River, and west to the Rihui Port. The area west of Rihui Port is considered to be the "rural line" area. The installation of telephones within five li west of Rihui Port requires a monthly rental of eight or ten yuan (compared to five or six yuan in non-rural areas), plus a line connection fee of two yuan per pole span. In areas where lines have not yet reached, an additional pole fee of five yuan per pole is required. Similar regulations exist in other areas, such as Zhabei and Jiangwan. This approach unduly restricts the use of telephones by residents in slightly remote areas, hindering development to a significant extent. It is urgently necessary to reform this and establish new regulations to ensure that all citizens within the same urban area enjoy equal treatment, so that telephone services can gradually become more widespread, and the Telephone Bureau's business can develop and its revenue can increase.

(2) Change or abolish the charging method for Sino-foreign calls. Currently, Chinese telephone subscribers who wish to speak with telephones in the concessions must first pay a fee for registration before they can make calls at any time. The same applies to concession subscribers calling Chinese areas. In reality, very few telephone subscribers register, which severely limits communication between Chinese and concession telephones, causing great inconvenience to citizens. Furthermore, a charge of five cents per call is too high. If it is possible to eliminate the call charge or reduce it to one or two cents per call, it would be beneficial to the development of the telephone business.

(3) Establish public telephones. All major cities in Europe and America have public telephones. Even within the concessions of this city, such facilities exist. Their convenience to the public is the same as rental cars and public water taps. This allows citizens who cannot afford to install private telephones to enjoy the convenience of telephones at a minimal cost. At the same time, the Telephone Bureau can increase its income. It is urgently necessary to install them widely, such as in prosperous locations such as Zhabei Baoshan Road, Datong Road, Hengfeng Road, Mongolia Road, Xinjiang Road, and Hubei Xiaodongmen, Xinbeimen, Laoximen.

(4) Recover the Songyang Telephone Company. Wusong is an important area of this city, and its future development is immeasurable. Its telephone business requires careful planning and improvement. The Songyang Telephone Company in that area is currently unable to improve due to lack of responsible personnel and excessive losses. It should be recovered at a fair price to facilitate rectification and unified authority.

(5) Establish a Pudong branch. The Pudong area is gradually prospering, and the need for telephones is very high. The few original Sino-foreign telephones that were installed have already expired and should be dismantled. Therefore, the establishment of a branch is truly urgent. Although it is heard that the Ministry of Communications also has this plan, it is not known when it will be realized.

(6) Establish more branches. Each telephone line is connected to only one machine. Therefore, to save materials and reduce malfunctions, it is advisable to establish more branches. Given the size of this city, there are only the Hubei Main Bureau, the Zhabei First and Second, and four branches in Jiangwan and Wusong. This is not economical in terms of materials. Furthermore, this city is developing very rapidly, and the original overhead wiring method is becoming difficult to cope with. In the future, it will be necessary to switch to underground lines. However, adopting underground lines will require even more branch stations. Although it is said that the Shanghai Telephone Bureau also plans to add a branch in the new western district, it is not known when it will be realized. Moreover, it is not only the new western district that needs it, but also suitable locations in Zhabei and Pudong should have more branches.

(7) Add trunk lines. The trunk lines between Nanshi and Zhabei and between them and the concessions have not been added for a long time. Currently, the number of calls is gradually increasing and is insufficient to meet demand. (For example, the number of Sino-foreign calls in 1927 was 623,000, and in 1929 it was 918,400.) As a result, when both parties call, it is often not possible to connect immediately due to the lack of available lines, which is extremely inconvenient. It is urgently necessary to add trunk lines to meet the needs.

(8) Rectify the lines. It is undeniable that there are many malfunctions in the Chinese telephone system in the city. The reason for this is often due to the poor quality of the line materials or poor construction. Even during major storms, other utility poles are not affected, but telephone poles and lines are the first to be damaged. Therefore, from a technical point of view, to rectify the Chinese telephone system in the city, it is advisable to first inspect the telephone lines and repair or renovate them separately, so that users do not frequently experience unreliable calls.

(9) Recover Sino-foreign telephones. The installation of Sino-foreign telephones in Chinese areas not only hinders the unification of the telephone business but also harms national sovereignty. Now that the contracts have expired, they should be recovered as soon as possible. Although the Ministry of Communications has said that it will lay lines as soon as the line materials are purchased and negotiate the recovery, the contracts have been expired for a long time, and no progress has been reported.

(10) Ban and recover foreign telephone companies on both sides of the road beyond the border. The installation of telephones by foreign merchants on both sides of the roads built beyond the border is as detrimental to national sovereignty as the supply of water and electricity by foreign merchants on both sides of the roads built beyond the border. Although the city's water and electricity business is commercially operated, after the Bureau urged them, the supply of water and electricity to foreign merchants on both sides of the roads built beyond the border has been gradually recovered for existing installations, and new installations are prohibited. However, the city's Chinese telephones have always been operated by the government, and no measures have been heard to ban and recover foreign telephone companies on both sides of the roads built beyond the border. It is urgently necessary to imitate the water and electricity measures to ban and recover them to protect sovereignty and maintain interests.

Request to Reduce Export Tax on Zhongshan Ge 100

▲ Submission from the Shanghai Silk Industry Association

The Shanghai Shengjing Silk Industry Association yesterday submitted a document to the Ministry of Industry, Commerce and Finance, stating that Sheng Chou Zhongshan Ge has suffered a sharp decline in sales due to the harsh taxation by the Shanghai Customs. They request a swift review and reduction of the customs export tax to seek relief and maintain the silk industry. Shengze in Suzhou has long been a major producer of Zhongshan Ge, which is entirely woven from rayon and cotton. This represents a painstaking effort to imitate foreign goods and recover rights. It is sufficient to resist the invasion of foreign goods from Japan and other countries externally, and to maintain the livelihoods of hundreds of thousands of industrial and commercial workers internally. In recent years, it has suddenly been subject to valuation and taxation by the Shanghai Customs, and the valuation is arbitrary, even exceeding the cost. Currently, the tax on one load of Zhongshan Ge has reached as high as 18 or 19 taels of silver. The increased costs make promotion difficult, production and sales are declining, and the livelihoods of workers are threatened. Thousands of merchants are closing businesses and workers are stopping machines. It is truly unbearable to describe. The customs export tax for textiles made of real silk and rayon or real silk and cotton is uniformly 5 taels and 5 mace per load. Now, the tax on textiles made of rayon and cotton is so harshly levied, how can the industry survive? Furthermore, the import tax on Japanese foreign goods is only 12.5% of the value, allowing them to be sold in various domestic trading ports. Due to the different tax rates and the disparity in costs between imported goods and domestic textiles, it is no wonder that foreign goods are increasingly flooding the market, while domestic goods are declining day by day. It is impossible to compete and resist.

Let us now consider the silk tax rate levied on Zhongshan Ge before it is exported, which is also quite substantial. For example, when rayon is imported from Shanghai, it is subject to an import tax of 12.5% of the value. When it is transported from Shanghai to Shengze, it is subject to a Likin tax of 5% of the value in Shengze. When it is woven and transported to Shanghai, it is subject to a production and sales tax of 5% of the value in Shengze. If we add the Shanghai Customs export tax of approximately 19% of the value, the tax on Zhongshan Ge in this province has reached a staggering 31.5% of the value. When transported to other provinces and countries, it is subject to taxation everywhere, an unparalleled burden. It is truly shocking to hear. In comparison, foreign silk is taxed once and can be sold throughout the country, regardless of the vast distances. If the tax rate on Zhongshan Ge is not reduced, there will be no way to resist foreign goods, and the silk industry will have no way to escape danger. This is directly related to the livelihoods of industrial and commercial workers, which is extremely important and significant. It is also indirectly related to the national treasury's tax revenue, which is also substantial. Therefore, we respectfully submit a request for a review of the reasons for reducing the customs export tax on Zhongshan Ge. We respectfully request that your ministry, in accordance with the utmost intention of promoting national goods, and mindful of the fact that our industry is in imminent danger, approve the customs export tax on rayon and cotton woven Zhongshan Ge to be taxed in the same way as rayon and real silk or real silk and cotton woven products, in order to show balance and maintain the silk industry, and await instructions for compliance, which will truly be for the public convenience.

Tragic Accident on Jiangwan Road During Qingming Festival 101

▲ Huang Manyi Visited Graves with Family

▲ Driving Over the Sports Association Road Bridge

▲ Collision Between a Car and a Bus While Avoiding a Small Vehicle

▲ Eight People in the Car Were Seriously Injured

Yesterday was the Qingming Festival, and people were traveling to the countryside to sweep graves in an endless stream. Those who lived far away hired cars for their convenience. It was not uncommon to see cars speeding along Jiangwan Road. A Cantonese man named Huang Manyi (who worked for China Travel Service) took his family, relatives, and friends, a total of seven people, to the Shanghai Public Cemetery in Jiangwan early yesterday morning to bury and sweep graves. They also used a car as transportation. When they drove to the bridge on Xitiyu Association Road, another car came head-on. In the urgency, they could not avoid it, and they collided. All eight people in Huang Manyi's car, including the driver, were injured. Three of Huang's female relatives were seriously injured. The car was also badly damaged. It was truly an unexpected disaster. The details are as follows:

▲ Two Cars Collided. Huang Manyi, a Cantonese, lives at No. 2 Wenyuanfang, Yokohama Bridge, North Sichuan Road. At around 5:30 yesterday morning, he, together with his relatives Lu Huang, Zheng Zhou, Huang, Huang Chen, Chen Yuexuan, Huang Yuan, and others, hired a car from Jiangwan Gongji Automobile Company at No. 15 Depeliri, East Yokohama Road, to go to Jiangwan to sweep graves. The car number was Shi 963, driven by Gu A'xiao, a native of Liuhe. Huang and the other seven people were crowded into the car, carrying offerings for their ancestors. When the car reached the Xitiyu Association Road bridge on Jiangwan Road and was going downhill, a car with the number Shi 953 (Concession 17580), driven by Yu Bingyan, a native of Yangzhou and a driver for the Tian Tian Automobile Company on Baek Road, suddenly came rushing towards them. At that time, there was a small car slowly moving forward in front of the car. Car No. 953, in order to move forward, went around the small car and drove forward in a semi-circular line. The car No. 963 on the bridge was already going downhill and wanted to avoid it, but the two cars collided. The people in the car were suddenly shocked, leaning forward and backward, and were instantly uneasy. At the same time, the car windows shattered, and their heads and faces were seriously injured.

▲ Eight People Injured. There were no passengers in car No. 953, and no one was injured. All seven passengers in car No. 963, including the driver, were injured. The names are as follows: Lu Huang, 35 years old, injured in the head; Li, 26 years old, injured in the face; Zheng Zhou, 52 years old, injured in the head, face, and abdomen; Huang Chen, 47 years old, injured in the head; Huang Manyi, 27 years old, injured in the mouth, waist, and legs; Chen Yuexuan, 62 years old, injured in the top of the head; Huang Yuan, 23 years old, injured in the chest. All were sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment. Among them, Lu Huang, Li, and Zheng Zhou were more seriously injured.

Unprecedented Tragedy: Westerner's Finger Severed and Tendons Pulled Out 102

▲ A Tragic Scene on Nanjing Road

▲ A Westerner Driving Carelessly

▲ Finger Severed and Tendons Pulled Out on the Gear Wheel

▲ Sent to the Hospital in Life-Threatening Condition

Yesterday afternoon around 4:00 PM, there were crowds of vehicles and horses and endless streams of pedestrians at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Zhejiang Road. At that time, a Westerner came speeding along on a motorcycle, his speed so fast that he seemed to disappear in an instant. The Westerner saw the green light shining brightly and was about to speed through when suddenly a red light appeared on the utility pole. The Westerner did not dare to violate the rules and immediately braked. However, the motorcycle was small, and the sudden braking caused the vehicle to swerve, and the Westerner fell to the ground. At the same time, his right thumb was caught in the chain of the wheel. The leather glove he was wearing was crushed. The Westerner tried to use his remaining strength to right his vehicle, but unexpectedly, the tendon in his thumb rotated with the wheel, got caught in the engine, and was pulled out for more than two feet. The Westerner could no longer endure it and immediately fainted, his face pale and blood flowing like a fountain. For a moment, pedestrians scrambled to watch the excitement. Nanjing Road was crowded with people. The police, fearing that there would be more trouble, dispersed the crowd and sent the Westerner to the Public Works Department Hospital for treatment in a police car. According to the doctor, his injuries were dangerous and his life was in danger. Because the Westerner was too seriously injured, he could not speak, so his name was not known in detail.

▲ Foes Meet and Handed Over to Police

It was not until May of last year that she managed to seize an opportunity to ask someone to send a letter to the owner of the Lv-owned inn, asking them to forward it to her grandmother to find a way to pull her out of the mire. Her grandmother received the letter and went to Pukou, but the prostitute had been moved by the madam to Yangzhou and hidden. After entrusting Director Zhou there to send a letter to Yangzhou, her niece was sent back to Pukou and handed over to her. The night before last, she passed by Yalu Road and unexpectedly met the defendant, so she handed her over to the police to be arrested. She requested punishment, etc. Then, Du A'bao's grandmother, Chen Du, arrived and testified that her niece had suddenly disappeared a few days before her wedding, and there was no news of her. Later, she received a letter from Lv, stating that she had been abducted and sold to a Pukou brothel. She went to Nanjing and begged Mr. Lv to go to Pukou to inquire at the Chen brothel. However, she was hidden by the madam in Yangzhou again. After entrusting Director Zhou there to send a letter to Yangzhou, her niece was sent back to Pukou and handed over to her, etc. When questioned, the defendant Cai Longyu stated that she and A'bao met while working in the silk factory. At the end of November the year before last, she heard that A'bao had eloped with her lover and was not abducted by her. The current statement is all false, etc. She also hired attorney Fu Kang to defend her. Judge Luo stated that the statements of the two parties were completely contradictory. The truth should be investigated. The defendant was ordered to be remanded in custody and the hearing was rescheduled to investigate the matter further.

One More Man in Bed 106

▲ Adulteress Still Trying to Deny Her Wrongdoings

▲ Husband Was Furious and Tried to Kill Her with a Knife

Chang Jinlong from Hebei lives in a thatched shed in Yu's Temple, Pudong. His wife, Chang Ji, is in her prime. She is from Jiangyin. She went out to do business the day before yesterday morning. Because it was raining, she returned home to get her leather shoes and saw a man in bed with his wife, their necks entwined. When he pulled back the covers, both of them were naked. He recognized the man as Ding Kaifa, a tinsmith from Wujin who lived next door. He was so consumed by jealousy that he grabbed a knife and slashed wildly, injuring Ding's wrist. Ding ran away naked, without even having time to put on his pants. At that time, the neighbors were all shocked and gathered. Chang then held a knife to kill his wife, but was stopped by the neighbors. Chang then reported the incident to the First Precinct of the Third District and accused her, presenting Ding's clothes, shoes, and socks as evidence. The police were dispatched to arrest Ding and the woman. The woman stated that when her husband went out, she had not gotten out of bed and was still in a good dream. She did not know how Ding Kaifa got into bed or how she was raped. She was only awakened when her husband came home and tried to kill her. The precinct chief said that unless someone was dead, it was impossible for someone to get into bed and commit adultery without her knowing. He ordered her to be detained. Ding Kaifa was asked and claimed that he had been having an affair with the woman for only a month and that this was only the second time they had engaged in adultery. The precinct chief reviewed the statements and determined that the case was clear. He ordered them to be sent to the District Court Prosecutor's Office for examination and ordered them to be detained for further investigation.

Xu Houyu Returns to Shanghai After Escaping Danger 107

▲ Abducted for Half a Year

On September 21 of last year, the Japan Mail Line's Osaka Company was robbed at sea off Shantou, losing tens of thousands of yuan. Before leaving, the pirates abducted four passengers on board for ransom. One of the four passengers was Xu Houyu, an employee of a British trading company in Shanghai, who was traveling to Xiamen on business and was abducted by the bandits. After the incident, the British Consul negotiated with the Guangdong provincial authorities for rescue. Xu's family also sent people to inquire in all directions. It was not until November that they received a ransom letter from the bandits. They also sent two representatives to Hong Kong to negotiate with the hostage's family, agreeing on 12,000 yuan. Later, the Guangdong-sent naval and police forces discovered the bandit's den on March 15th and attacked. After a fierce battle with the bandits for three days, the bandits were defeated and fled in all directions. Xu Houyu, who was held in the bandit's nest, and Taiwanese hostage Huang took advantage of the fact that the bandits had gone out to fight and there was no one guarding them, and risked their lives to escape amidst the hail of bullets. At that time, they were not familiar with the roads and were worried about being captured by the bandits again, so they hid during the day and traveled at night. They were without food for three days. Xu Huang ate potatoes and grass roots to fill their stomachs. After escaping from the bandit's den, they traveled on mountain roads for eight days and eight nights before finally finding a village. The two had fainted for several hours on the way. Fortunately, they were rescued by villagers who gave them food and water. They arrived in Hong Kong on March 27th. Huang stayed in Hong Kong to go to Taiwan, while Xu took a boat to Shanghai. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday. In total, he had been abducted for half a year and imprisoned in the bandit's den for about three months. In the first two months, he was moved by the bandits every night, so his hands and feet were covered in calluses and he suffered terribly. It is now heard that after returning home, he will go to the hospital for treatment.

Sailor of the Water Police Pingyang Battleship Contracted the Epidemic 108

▲ Initial Symptoms Were Vomiting Blood

▲ Soon Collapsed and Died

Gong Mianqin, the captain of the 17th Detachment of the 4th District of the Jiangsu Water Police, took the Pingyang Battleship to patrol the waters of Chongming and Qidong counties. The ship was near Xiaheisha at around 3 PM the day before yesterday when suddenly a water policeman on the ship fell ill, vomiting blood. He immediately collapsed on the deck and soon died. Shortly afterwards, several policemen contracted the same illness, vomiting blood one after another and collapsing on the ship. One of them was unconscious, while the others were still conscious. Captain Gong immediately sent a doctor to treat them, who observed that the symptoms were sudden and severe, and determined that it was an acute infectious disease, which was extremely dangerous. However, he did not know what kind of epidemic it was. The ship then sailed to Chongming yesterday morning and took the sick to Chongming Hospital for treatment. At the same time, the entire ship was disinfected to prevent the spread of the epidemic.

Zhabei Kunming Yuxin Two Li 109

▲Changed to Connect to Chinese Territory Tap Water

Yuxin Li, located on Kunming Road, Dixiwei Road, Zhabei, was previously supplied with water by the Shanghai Waterworks Company. However, at that time, there were no Zhabei water pipes in the area, so it could not be implemented. Recently, the company completed the laying of pipes in a section of Oujia Road. Vehicle Licenses Issued by the Public Works Department 110

▲Increase in Automobiles

▲Shoulder Carriers Gone

According to the Continental Daily, the means of transportation in Shanghai have been increasing in recent years. For example, in 1920, there were only 1,899 automobiles.
