Municipal Public Security Bureau 111

Banning the Burning of Paper Ingots During Qingming Festival

Yesterday (the 5th) was the traditional Qingming Festival. Some women carried paper ingots, grass, etc., to guild halls to burn and pay respects. Yuan, the director of the Shanghai Special Municipal Public Security Bureau, noted that there were numerous guild halls and public offices in the areas south of the Shanghai city and in Zhabei. The burning of paper ingots by the people not only wasted useful money, but also posed a fire hazard due to the densely packed thatched houses, which are dry and easily ignited. Once a fire breaks out, it could repeat last year's incident in Pudong, greatly hindering local security. At a time when superstitions are being eliminated, it is necessary to strictly prohibit such activities. Yesterday, he issued a special order to the 2nd, 4th, and 5th districts and all sub-bureaus to dispatch additional police officers to the various guild halls and public offices within their jurisdictions, such as those in the south of Shanghai, Siming, Huining, Hunan, Hubei, Dongting, Dongshan, Jinting, Jiangxi, Chao Hui, etc., and in Zhabei, Xijin, Huaiyang, Jianghuai, Wujiang, Wujin, Haichang, Guangzhao, Yanxu, Huzhou, etc., as well as places where coffins are stored. Police officers were stationed at each location throughout the day to maintain order. Those who encountered stubborn and ignorant people should be persuaded with kind words to eliminate superstition, it was said.

Sand Junk "Guo Changhe" Encountered Pirates 112

▲The Ship and Three Helmsmen Were Taken

▲Crew Members Shot and Driven Away

The Shandong Nuguo sand junk named "Guo Changhe," which was carrying cotton cloth and yarn from Yuren Gong and other firms, was sailing on the Qingkou Sea on the 27th of last month when it was suddenly attacked by a large group of pirates. The pirates arrived in two stolen ships, carrying weapons, and ordered the "Guo Changhe" to stop. Upon seeing this, the "Guo Changhe" tried to escape, but the pirates opened fire, wounding three crew members. The crew members, panicked by the situation, allowed the pirates to do as they pleased. The pirates swarmed onto the ship and searched everywhere. Finding no large amount of silver, the pirates became angry and, after beating the shipowner, forced him to sail to the foot of a mountain by the sea. They then drove the more than twenty crew members on board ashore and seized the ship, leaving three helmsmen on board to navigate.

Page 16

The two pirate ships followed closely behind and sailed towards the east coast. The crew members who had been driven ashore walked for a day and night before reaching Nuguo, where they reported the incident to the goods firms. The shipowner and the three wounded crew members were sent to a hospital. One crew member died from his injuries. The ship's boss, accompanied by half of the crew members, took a steamer to Shanghai to report the incident to Yuren Gong and other firms. The firms have now telegraphed the local naval and land authorities to strictly suppress the pirates. It is reported that the goods on board the ship were worth more than 50,000 taels of silver, and the Nuguo firms have been telegraphed to investigate the whereabouts of the ship, it was said.

The training time should not interfere with the public's occupations. According to the above methods, the cost is limited, but the results are significant. The museum is required to immediately start the process and report the progress of the process at any time, it was said.

Municipal Public Utilities Bureau Formulates Regulations 122

for Business Rickshaw Donation and License

The operating rickshaw licenses in this city have always been in the name of the substitute donor, with the license number of each vehicle listed under the name. Therefore, this type of license is only used for donating money, and several vehicles share one license, which is slightly different from other types of vehicle licenses. Now that the licenses issued in the previous period have expired, the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, in order to facilitate the businesses and show distinction, has specifically changed the name of this type of license to the "Shanghai Special City Business Rickshaw Donation License" and set rules and

regulations. Branches, private self-defense weapons, unless it is extremely dangerous, when you have to take self-defense measures, are not allowed to be opened; Article 8, this gun license, no matter when and where, must not be separated from the gun (bullet), such as encountering Chinese Customs police checkpoints Then Article 9, has been submitted to the City Government for record and implementation, and now the rules and regulations will be explored and recorded as follows: (1) Anyone with 5 or more rickshaws for business can

Apply for this license alone; (2) In addition to its own vehicles, the owner of the vehicle may also include other people's rickshaws for business as a substitute donation; (3) The owner of the vehicle represents other business rickshaws to donate, and the number of its own vehicles must be at least three, and the number of cars for substitute donation must be at least twelve, totaling at least fifteen; (4) If the number of its own cars reported by the owner of the car is falsely stated, once verified, the license shall be canceled immediately; (5) The owner of the car shall pay the monthly donation to the Tax Collection Office of the Finance Bureau before the 15th of each month according to the number of cars reported (including self-owned donations), and shall not be short; (6) All responsibilities of the vehicles reported by the owner of the car (including his own and substitute donations) shall be fully borne by the person who pays the donation; (7) The owner of the car shall abide by all the regulations in this city related to rickshaws for business; (8) When the Bureau makes inquiries to the owner of the car within the scope of its duties, the owner of the car shall not disobey; (9)

The restrictions in Articles 1 and 3 of these Rules shall not apply to rickshaws for business in the Pudong municipal area for the time being.

Foreigners Applying for Gun Licenses 123

▲Must Comply with Regulations

The Municipal Government previously approved the consultation from the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs, which issued the Provisional Regulations for Foreigners Residing in China to Apply for Self-Defense Gun Licenses. Yesterday, it sent separate letters to the consuls of various countries in Shanghai and issued instructions to the Branch Security Bureau to review and verify the self-defense gun licenses and the licensing offices to comply with the regulations. The regulations are as follows: Article 1: When foreigners traveling or residing in China carry self-defense guns (including hunting guns), they shall apply for a gun license. The procedures for applying for a license shall be in accordance with these regulations. Article 2: When foreigners apply for a gun license, they shall first obtain an application form from the nearby county (city) government, and specify the nationality, name, occupation, gun type, number, and quantity, and have the nearby consul of that country sign and guarantee it. Together with a photo and fee, and the gun(s) they are carrying, they shall submit it to the county (city) government for verification and forward it to the provincial (special city) government for approval and issuance of the license. If the applicant for a gun license is a diplomatic personnel stationed in China by various countries, they may directly request the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to request the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs to approve and issue the license. Article 3: This gun license shall be one license for each gun. No license shall be issued for multiple guns together. Article 4: Each person shall be allowed to carry one self-defense gun and 200 rounds of ammunition. Hunters may carry an additional hunting gun, but must apply for a separate gun license. Article 5: When applying for a gun license, five two-and-a-half-inch photos shall be submitted. The photo fee is two yuan for new-style guns and one yuan for old-style guns (the distinction between new and old shall refer to the Regulations for Issuing Self-Defense Guns and Artillery to Nationals). If the applicant is a diplomatic personnel stationed in China by various countries, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs may consider the situation and request a waiver of fees. Article 6: Foreigners who have been licensed shall not alter the name or other gun types on the license, nor shall they replace or forge it. Article 7: Self-defense guns shall not be fired unless it is extremely dangerous and self-defense measures must be taken. Article 8: This gun license shall not be separated from the gun (ammunition) at any time or place. When encountering a checkpoint or military police checkpoint, it shall be immediately handed over for verification. If there are no suspicious circumstances, it shall be returned to the original person after verification. Article 9: If it is found that the gun carried does not match the gun listed on the gun license, or if the appearance differs from the photo on the gun license, the gun may be confiscated and the gun license canceled. Article 10: If a licensed foreigner violates the gun license regulations or other illegal acts, the local authorities may detain the person and the gun together and report it for investigation. Article 11: This gun license shall not be valid in areas that have been notified and travel has been stopped. Article 12: This regulation shall be valid for one year and shall expire thereafter. Article 13: This regulation shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Municipal Land Bureau Bans 124

Buying Land Under False Company Names

The Shanghai Special Municipal Land Bureau, in view of the fact that impersonating a company name for land transactions can easily lead to disputes over property rights, has specifically met with the distribution offices of various movable property deeds. In the future, if anyone requests a deed for buying land in the name of a company, they must first verify the registration certificate. When paying taxes and transferring ownership to the Land Bureau, they must also present the registration certificate to avoid disputes over property rights caused by impersonating a company name, it was said.

Report of the Tragic Disaster Situation in Yuxian County 126

Zhou Xiaofan, the representative of the Henan Provincial Government Relief Association stationed in Shanghai, recently received a report from the Yuxian County Chamber of Commerce Cao Jinming and the executive committee member of the county party headquarters, Hou Zhenting, regarding the disaster situation in the county. The report stated that Yuxian County is a famous county in Henan Province, a gathering place for drug merchants, and has always been known for its prosperity. Since the city was captured by the huge bandit Bai Lang in May of the Republic, and a large-scale plunder was carried out, the city and rural merchants have lost all their wealth. Since then, bandits have been as numerous as hairs, burning, killing, looting, and there has been no peaceful day. In the autumn of the 13th year, Cao Shiying, the Shaanxi army, led thousands of undisciplined soldiers to garrison in Yu, using their power to demand more than 500,000 yuan in supplies and military pay, and colluded with the bandits to disturb the four villages. The people of Yu were on the verge of bankruptcy. In the spring of the 14th year, the brigade mutinied for no reason, looting, burning and killing, which was extremely miserable. In the spring of the 15th year, the brigade withdrew westward, and then Li Zhenya led tens of thousands of bandits to Yu to eat, demanding more than 70,000 yuan from merchants and civilians every month to pay for their military pay, and separately demanding firewood, grass, rice, and noodles worth tens of thousands of yuan per day. The army was stationed for more than a year, demanding a total of 1.5 million yuan, and their officers and soldiers were all from the green forest, colluding with the bandits, so the banditry in the four villages increased day by day, and the private losses were even greater than the levies. In the 16th year, after the Second Army Group defeated the bandit troops, the famous bandits Li Geng and others rose up at the time, with 6,000 to 7,000 bandits, killing everyone they met and burning every house they saw. All the villages in the four villages were attacked and broken, and the farmers who had not been killed all fled. The villages and fields were turned into wasteland. The villages dozens of miles west of the county were uninhabited. The banditry was at its worst. Unfortunately, in the 17th year, there was another severe drought, and there was no grass in the fields. The victims searched for food and stone flour to fill their hunger. They often ran around all day without getting anything. They were truly unable to protect themselves in the morning and did not know where they would die in the evening. There were suicides due to starvation everywhere, and it was even more difficult to count the exact number. When the rain fell in the summer of last year, the autumn crops could be planted. When the people of Yu were celebrating that there was already a chance of survival, unexpectedly, a flood broke out, and residents along the Ying River were washed away, and good land was turned into sand and gravel, with losses estimated at more than 5 million yuan. Before the flood had subsided, the huge bandit Wei Zhi and others led more than 10,000 followers to rob the villages in the southeast of the county, from a few miles outside the city to the Huangyu Store, Southwest Wang, and other villages 60 miles southwest of the county, and the towns of Shen etc. All the villages in the town were robbed. Therefore, the whole county was a place for the bandits to gallop around. The houses in large and small villages were almost burnt down. Those with a little property were taken away, and those who were poor and had no money were often massacred. The villagers were terrified and fled into the county town to beg for food, filling the streets and lanes. They could only rely on begging and could not live. There was no place where people were starving to death on the streets. Alas, the people of Yu suffered so much that they were in such a miserable situation. They only hoped that the years would be peaceful and the fields would be bountiful, which could make up for the losses by one in ten thousand. Suddenly, more than 100,000 central troops suddenly arrived in the county, and then fought with the Northwest Army in the western half of the city for more than ten days. The supply of vehicles and fodder was exhausted. As soon as the war subsided, Liu Guitang's army, the 4th Division of the newly compiled army, stayed in the county town, and the county people were ordered to apportion all the military pay and supplies. If there was any delay, they would be forced to act freely. In the county for more than a month, a total of 424,000 yuan was levied. Last month, when the army was about to leave, the city was closed for several days, and every household was searched. All the soft rice and food of the merchants and people were emptied, and their value was about 60,000. The people who were dying were subjected to another severe robbery. The deep water and fire could not be described their suffering.

Continued Request for Spring Relief from Representatives of Langxi County 127

According to the reports from Anhui Langxi County representatives Niao Huinan, Wang Jing, and others, the spring disaster was severe, and there was no way to survive without relief. Now, according to the continued report from the representatives, the 10,000 famished victims in the county were displaced, and the whole family of several people poisoned themselves and died, and the thieves and bandits were even more committed to robbing and dividing the spoils, only to get one or two pieces of meat and thousands of copper coins, and they were immediately executed by the officials, and the suicides were increasing in an endless stream, and the offenders were increasing one after another, so they would not do that if they were happy. Now the wheat is half-frozen to death due to too much rain and snow, and even the seedlings are eaten by the victims, and those who planted seeds have nothing to gain, and the autumn harvest is difficult to expect. With 200,000 victims, if they don't die, they will be thieves and bandits. Some people know that your association is relieving Shaanxi, Henan, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang provinces, and taking care of them is not against the law, but our county is severely affected, and the area is not large, so less relief money will be more effective. In this shortest period of time, if we can allocate 30,000 yuan in cash to relieve the planting, we can still do it. If we miss the time, there will be no effect in spring and autumn, even if it is a huge sum of 100,000 or 200,000 yuan. We sincerely ask you to show your sympathy and lend a helping hand, and we will be waiting for your order.

Wang did not avoid it and continued to walk forward, intending to cross the road, and was struck by the car. He fell to the road and was injured by the rear wheel of the vehicle. Officer No. 2301 took Wang to Tongren Hospital, but he died of his injuries yesterday afternoon. The hospital reported this to the Mixed Court, which ordered detectives to take Wang's body to the forensic examination office on Fielun Road. Yesterday morning at 10:45, the Special District Court dispatched Prosecutor Guo Wei to the scene to conduct an examination. The French detective explained the situation and stated that the driver of the car, Lu Jianian, was not present for questioning. According to Lu Jianian's statement, there were four workers in the car that day, and he was sitting in the front. The child was hit by the side of the car, and he did not see it. Later, he heard the workers say that a child had been injured. When he stopped the car, it was too late. He has been a driver for a year and a half. Ye Xiaolin stated that after Wang was hit, he immediately wrote a letter to his hometown, asking his parents to come to Shanghai. Therefore, he cannot make decisions about Wang's burial alone and must wait for his parents to arrive. After reviewing the statements, Prosecutor Guo announced that the hearing would be postponed to Monday next week.

Thieves Also Form Gangs 132

Dong Changgui, a Jiangbei native residing at 771 Yuanfang Road, along with Jiang Wenkui, Lu Zirong, Yu Maomao, and others, organized a gang of thieves within the International Settlement, stealing property from various businesses and residences. They were apprehended yesterday by Chief Detective Su Changsheng of the Huishan Police Station and taken back to the station. The head detective ordered them to be detained while the case was investigated and then sent to the Special District Court for trial.

Uncle-in-Law Commits Incest with Niece 133

▲Wei Gengsheng Violates Ethical Principles

Yan Xiaobao from Gaoyou had a sister who married Wei Gengsheng, a fellow villager. After a few years, the sister passed away. Later, Wei came to Shanghai to work at the power plant and lived at 117 Haichang Road in Zhabei. Last year, Wei returned to his hometown. Yan entrusted his biological daughter, Cui Bao (Wei's niece, 21 years old), to Wei to take to Shanghai to find work and supplement the family income. After Wei brought Cui Bao to Shanghai, he found her attractive and did not find her work but instead had sexual relations with her. This was discovered by Wei's mistress, Ms. Xu, leading to jealousy and forcing Wei to kick Cui Bao out and forbidding him from seeing her. Wei had no choice but to flee with Cui Bao to a workshop in Caojiadu in western Shanghai. They both worked in a yarn factory, living together like husband and wife. Wei's mistress was furious after Wei hid away. Cui Bao's father, Yan Xiaobao, came to Shanghai to look for Cui Bao because he had not heard from her since she arrived. He met Wei's mistress, Ms. Xu, who revealed that Wei and Cui Bao were having an affair and had fled. Yan was outraged that his uncle-in-law had committed incest with his niece, violating ethical principles. He searched everywhere and learned from a fellow villager that Wei and Cui Bao were working at a yarn factory in Caojiadu. He went there yesterday and waited outside the factory. At 6 p.m., he saw Wei and Cui Bao leaving the factory together. Yan tried to apprehend them, but Wei escaped. Yan had no choice but to report to the Second Precinct of the Fourth District and request their assistance in arresting him.

Daughter's Disappearance Leads to Dispute 134

▲Both Sides Engage in a Major Brawl

Wang Youyu, a native of Gaoyou, rented a place near the Sanjing Pier in Pudong and worked as a stevedore. Wang had a 19-year-old daughter who worked in a cigarette factory, leaving in the morning and returning in the evening, as usual. Unexpectedly, she disappeared on the sixth day of last month and has been missing for over a month. Wang's wife, Chen, suspected that Huang Kaitai, the son of their neighbor Huang Si from Changzhou, had abducted her. Yesterday, Wang's wife questioned Yang, Huang's wife, and a disagreement led to a conflict. Then, more people arrived on both sides, wielding weapons and fighting. As a result, both sides suffered minor injuries, but Wang had blood all over his face and was seriously injured. Officers from the Third Precinct of the Public Security Bureau arrived and arrested ten people, including Wang Si and his wife Yang, Wang Kaitai, Wang Youyu, Wang Chen, Zhang Huairen, Tang Lanxi, Wang Yang, Wang Si's son, and Wei Huang. After questioning by the district chief, the case was deemed criminal and referred to the District Court for prosecution in the afternoon.

Chen Bingjin Certainly Died by Suicide 135

Regarding the case of Chen Bingjin, a Jiangbei native, who died across from the World Cinema on Qingyun Road in Zhabei, his uncle Chen Zihong noticed rope marks on the back of the deceased's neck, different from those caused by hanging, and suspected foul play. He requested the District Court to conduct an examination, as reported yesterday. It is now known that the result of the examination by Prosecutor Lei and the coroner was that Chen died by suicide. Although there were marks on the back of his neck, they were caused when he hanged himself by wrapping the rope twice around his neck, resulting in the marks being higher in the front and lower in the back. If he had been strangled, the marks would have been the same shape in the front and back. The family accepted the findings. It is said that Chen Bingjin committed suicide because he was beaten after losing money gambling.

Prohibition of Hubei Limin Lottery 136

▲City Government Orders Public Safety and Social Affairs Bureaus to Investigate and Strictly Prohibit

The City Government considers the issuance of lotteries to be a form of gambling, disrupting finances and harming society. The Central Government has issued a clear order to prohibit them. However, some merchants and ruffians take advantage of the concessions, disregard the law, and continue to issue them to deceive the public. The Shanghai Executive Committee sent a letter to the City Government yesterday, stating that it had received a letter from Wang Lianqing, claiming that the Hubei Limin Lottery was a complete scam. Upon receiving the letter, the City Government immediately instructed the Public Safety Bureau to work with the Social Affairs Bureau to investigate and strictly prohibit it.

Committing Suicide in the River Due to Occasional Frustration 137

▲Foolish to the Name

▲Treating Life as Child's Play

Yesterday morning around 6:00 a.m., a man jumped into the river from the Baidu Bridge outside the Suzhou Creek mouth. He was spotted by Officer No. 24 of the Water Police, who rescued him. He claimed to be Xu Jigen, 45 years old, from Ningbo, residing at 39 Tongkang Lane, Holy Mother's Church Road. He has a 15-year-old daughter, and his wife, Zhu, works as a helper. He used to work as a laundry delivery man for Wang Zhangji Laundry on Jupiter Road. Because he only has a daughter, he leaves early and returns late. However, the owner has no way to make a living, so he committed suicide by jumping into the river. The head detective, after hearing his statement, ordered detectives to inquire at Wang Zhangji Laundry to see if Xu had been fired. The owner said that Xu's work had always been accurate, and he had not been fired. The detective reported this to the head detective, who then summoned his wife, Zhu, to the station. She said that her husband had the mindset of a child and would do pointless things if things did not go his way, like a fool. Since his wife had arrived, the head detective released Xu to her.

Grass Shed on Yinggui Road Catches Fire 138

▲Forty-Four Rooms Destroyed

Yesterday morning around 10:45, a grass shed at the intersection of Yinggui Road and Changchun Road in the jurisdiction of the First Precinct of the Fifth District of Zhabei caught fire. The fire spread for about 20 minutes, destroying 44 grass houses. The cause of the fire was careless cooking. A woman from Gaoyou named Wang Xu was taken to the precinct for investigation.

Fire at Baoshan Road 139

▲Lawyer Fei Guoxi's Residence Suffers

Yesterday morning around 9:00, a fire broke out in the upstairs厢房 of the residence of lawyer Fei Guoxi at 47 Shengsun Lane, Baoshan Road, Zhabei. Sparks flew and smoke filled the air. However, Fei and his family had left Shanghai a few days ago and had not returned for two days. The door was locked, and the maids were all downstairs, so they did not notice. The neighbors noticed and exclaimed that there was no one upstairs, so where was the fire coming from? Looking into the courtyard, it was already raging. They panicked and were at a loss. Fortunately, fire trucks from the Chinese and foreign concessions arrived and the firefighters rushed upstairs, broke down the door, and threw the burning clothes trunks and other items out the window and cut off the power lines, preventing further damage. The remaining fire was extinguished, and the patrolling police reported to the police station for investigation.

Floating Corpse on Nanjing Road Bund 140

Yesterday afternoon at 2:00, an unidentified male corpse suddenly floated to the surface of the river at the Nanjing Road Bund. He was wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants, had a monk's hairstyle, and was about 40 years old. The Western officer of the Water Police found the body and took it back to the police station, then turned it over to the Rescue Bureau for identification and preliminary burial, to facilitate the search for relatives to claim the body.

Chu Minyi Donates Salary to Support Fusheng Hospital 141

Commissioner Chu Minyi has spared no effort in social welfare undertakings in recent years. As he is about to go to Belgium, he has visited various social organizations and medical institutions in the city. He visited Fusheng Hospital at the intersection of Old Baz Road and Fusheng Road in Shanghai with his wife in the afternoon. Impressed by the hospital's perfect treatment tools, such as sunlight lamps, thermotherapy machines, and X-rays, as well as its charitable work, which provides free treatment to hundreds of poor people every day, he generously donated his salary monthly to support the charity's activities.

Yuyuan Calligraphy and Painting Charity Association Lottery Today 142

The Calligraphy and Painting Charity Association at 151 Yuyuan Road, Shanghai, was founded during the Xuantong reign of the Qing Dynasty. It has been operating until now with remarkable achievements. In order to raise funds, they issued calligraphy and painting tickets. This time, they solicited works from famous artists in Shanghai, all of which are exquisite, such as Zeng Nongran, Zhu Guwei, Yu Youren, Wang Yiting, Shen Xinhai, Cheng Yaosheng, and other seniors, who have all made great contributions. All the works have been carefully matched with gifts under public supervision, so ticket buyers are extremely enthusiastic. The lottery will be drawn today, and there will certainly be a grand occasion.

Lost Woman Crying on the Road 143

Zhao Yujie, 31 years old, from Yancheng, who lives in the north of the dog track on Jiaozhou Road in western Shanghai, and his tenant, Zhang Qi, 59 years old, from Funing, saw a girl about 10 years old wandering and crying on the road on the 10th of this month. They took her home. When asked her name, she said her name was Gen Di, 10 years old, from Funing, but she didn't answer the other questions. She stayed for three days without anyone claiming her. They dared not keep her for long, so yesterday, together with the landlord, they sent the child to the Sixth District Police Station for further processing.

Gray Greyhound Awaiting Collection 144

▲New New Company Workers' Union Cries of Unemployed Workers To all dear compatriots, our capitalist, New New Company, took advantage of the Lunar New Year to fire 43 of our fellow workers without any reason. We are all old employees who entered the company when it opened, especially those who came from Sincere and Wing On. The original intention was to earn a few more dollars, but who knew that we would suffer from internal disputes within the company, resulting in economic losses. However, we always felt that the cost of living was high and it was not easy to make a living, so we always kept calm and held on to our jobs during these years. Not to mention that we have made contributions, we feel that we have not made any mistakes. However, the company, without asking right from wrong, used its usual trick to treat workers and fired us in large numbers. We are citizens under the clear blue sky and white sun, protected by the party, and we cannot bear to be trampled on by capitalists as in the warlord era. Therefore, we reported the capitalist's unreasonable dismissal to the party and government agencies for assistance. Unexpectedly, the capitalist used the concession as a protective charm, listened to the instigation of one or two people, and ignored the government's orders. The Social Affairs Bureau convened three mediation sessions, but he ignored them all, regardless of our livelihood panic and the shame of our poverty. Today, in the autumn of expensive rice prices and difficult living, those who pay attention to social conditions are worried about the increasing number of unemployed people. New New capitalist, with huge assets, has a special intention to take advantage of this opportunity to fire a large number of workers, hoping to create social unemployment terror and trap workers in a desperate situation. We don't know what his intention is. We have been unemployed for more than two months, and our living difficulties are unbearable. We can only beg for help from all walks of life, hoping that the public will give us a fair judgment, so that the future of the labor movement can still be saved. Signed by 43 workers fired by the New New Company Workers' Union at the end of the year, April 5.

Weather Report 146

The Xujiahui Observatory forecast yesterday at 4:30 p.m. that the sky is overcast and changing. Low-pressure centers are lingering in Sichuan, Manchuria, Kyushu, and Luzon. There are extremely unstable breezes between these low-pressure areas. There is light fog along the coast. The highest temperature in Shanghai in the 24 hours before 3:00 p.m. yesterday was 6.4.4, and the lowest was 3.7.4. On the same day last year, the highest was 69.8 and the lowest was 42.6.

Scene at the Venue 148

Time flies like an arrow. Yesterday was the fifth day since the opening of the Games. The weather was sunny, and the spring atmosphere was rich. It was also the traditional Qingming Festival, so there were more spectators than usual. Among the events, the all-around competition had as many as eleven events. The ball games were all in the second round, so there was no empty space in the stands. Whenever the competitions were fierce, there was applause, cheers, and thunderous cheers. The athletes were all in high spirits, especially in the ball game competitions. In addition to the special records of each event, the news from the venue is recorded as follows:

▲Orderly

The order of the Games has been rectified for several days, so it has become more cautious. The military police are still guarding each exit. The police from the Public Security Bureau are directing traffic and maintaining order on the roads around the venue. The Party and Army of the First Regiment of the Salt Affairs Middle School is responsible for maintaining order in each sports ground inside the venue, and the Municipal Hospital is responsible for rescue. The order of each venue is well maintained.

▲Convenient Transportation

In addition to the fact that you can reach the Games directly by rickshaw from various places, the Highway Bureau has specially provided special cars at the City Station and New City Market to carry passengers. The cost yesterday was very economical. From the City Station to the Games, it only costs half a dime, and from the New City Market to the Games, it costs one dime. The bus runs once every ten minutes, and each round trip is full of passengers.

▲Visiting Groups

Yesterday, the visiting groups included 58 students from the Navigation Department of the Merchant Shipping Bureau Public School, led by Instructor Shi Weijun. Also (1) Shanghai East Asia Sports College 100 people, (2) Liangzhe Sports College 100 people, (3) Xunyu School 18 people, (4) Wuxi Middle School 25 people, (5) Shanghai Southeast Medical College 20 people, (6) Shanghai Minzhi Middle School Boy Scouts 60 people (7) Shanghai Minzhi Middle School 122 people, (8) Fudan University 126 people, (9) China University Law School 14 people (10) Nanjing Dongfang Public School 36 people, (11) Nanjing Jinling Girls' School 20 people, (12) Fudan Middle School 15 people, (13) Nanjing Huiwen Girls' School 30 people, (14) Labor University 160 people, (15) Tongji University Engineering College 20 people, (16) Shanghai Middle School High School Department 20 people, (17) Various schools, groups, and institutions in this province and city totaled more than 30,000 people.

▲Number of Tickets Sold

There were many finals the day before yesterday, so the audience was very enthusiastic. The number of tickets sold at each ticket office was: (1) Track and field stadium 3,153 tickets, 5,092 dimes; (2) Football stadium 795 tickets, 1,590 dimes; (3) Basketball stadium 1,484 tickets, 2,960 dimes, 65 tickets, 130 yuan. A total of 5,569 tickets were sold, totaling 946.1 yuan.

▲US Consul Visits

The US Consul in Shanghai, Mr. He Sidun, his wife, son and two others, came to Hangzhou from Shanghai yesterday (the 5th) to visit the Games. He attended a lunch hosted by Mayor Zhou Xiangxian at noon, and then went to the Games in Mayor Zhou's car. He was received by Mr. Wu Jianying, an official of the Games, and led to the track and field stadium for a week. He then went to the command stand. Mr. He praised all the facilities of the Games.

The Intensity of the 1600-Meter Relay Race 154

▲Liaoning Overtakes Shanghai in the Final Lap

▲Liu Changchun Strives to Create a New Record

▲Result: 3 Minutes, 42.5 Seconds

First: Liaoning::::Second: Shanghai

Third: Hunan::::Fourth: East Special District

Yesterday at 2 PM, the final of the men's 1600-meter relay race took place. Only four teams participated: Shanghai, Liaoning, Hunan, and East Special District. Teams from Tianjin, Beiping, Guangdong, and Zhejiang did not compete. It was heard that the Tianjin team was too fatigued from consecutive days of competition and was preparing to participate in today's 800-meter relay race, hence their absence. The audience's attention was focused on the Shanghai and Liaoning teams, as their strengths were considered equal, and it was uncertain who would emerge victorious. The Shanghai team lineup was Zhu Ruihong in the first leg, He Debao in the second leg, Su Zuqing in the third leg, and Wang Jianwu in the anchor leg. The Liaoning team lineup was Cai Fangpu in the first leg, Gu Shirong in the second leg, Lang Dakui in the third leg, and the sprinting prodigy Liu Changchun in the anchor leg.

▲Shanghai Takes the Lead

At the sound of the starting gun, Cai Fangpu of Liaoning sprinted out, leading the way. Zhu Ruihong of Shanghai was second, East Special District third, and Hunan fourth. By the halfway point, Zhu Ruihong was making a strong effort to catch up, closing the gap with Cai to about one meter. By 300 meters, Zhu and Cai were neck and neck. Eventually, Zhu took first place, with Cai of Liaoning second, a few steps behind. East Special District remained third, and Hunan fourth.

▲A Three-Meter Gap

In the second leg, He Debao of the Shanghai team ran hard, with Gu Shirong of the Liaoning team closely following. Both maintained their positions. However, in the final half of the lap, He Debao had a slight advantage, with a three-meter gap between first and second place. East Special District was third, and Hunan fourth.

▲During the Third Leg

In the third leg, Su Zuqing of the Shanghai team became even more spirited, while Lang Dakui of the Liaoning team did not show weakness, chasing hard. Ultimately, Shanghai was faster during the baton exchange, further widening the gap. By the time they reached the end of the leg, the distance between first and second was about five meters. Everyone believed that Shanghai would undoubtedly win the championship, and Liaoning, despite its ferocity, could not touch it. Unexpectedly, the result was quite surprising.

▲The Prodigy Displays His Power

In the fourth leg, Wang Jianwu of the Shanghai team knew that a strong opponent was behind him and that extraordinary effort was needed to complete the mission. He pushed hard, but Liu Changchun, the sprinting prodigy in the anchor leg for Liaoning, advanced fiercely, swift as a galloping horse. By the time he ran 200 meters, the gap was only three meters. By 300 meters, Shanghai and Liaoning were side by side. At 320 meters, he completely overtook, and a burst of applause shook eardrums. At the finish line, Liu Changchun was about three meters ahead of Wang Jianwu, creating a new record of 3 minutes and 42.5 seconds. (Note: The national record is 3 minutes and 45.4 seconds.) Liaoning's victory was entirely due to the prodigy's power. Without the prodigy, it would have been impossible to surpass Wang Jianwu by seven or eight meters. At the time, Hunan also overtook, East Special District took third, and East Special District fourth.

Soccer 155

Second Round, Group Two

(1) Shanghai Overwhelms Hubei

▲A Score of Nine to One

▲Hubei, Though Defeated, Deserves Honor

Li Huitang Did Not Play

(2) Guangdong Defeats Jiangxi

▲A Score of Twelve to Zero

▲Victory Comes Quite Easily

▲The Shanghai vs. Hubei Match

The Shanghai team has many talented players and has reigned supreme in Shanghai for more than a year. The excellence of their soccer skills is widely praised by people throughout the country, requiring no introduction from reporters. The Hubei team's technique is ordinary. As a newly formed team facing a battle-hardened force, their chances of not being defeated were slim. Watching yesterday's game, the Hubei team strived hard from beginning to end, never losing heart due to setbacks, and regarded the competition as an opportunity to hone their skills. This spirit is truly rare in the sports world, and the team can take pride in it. Hubei team, keep up the effort!

Shanghai Scores Too Many Goals 156

At the afternoon hour, the two teams began contact. The Shanghai team advanced steadily, while the Hubei team's formation was very scattered, leading to a complete rout. Initially, the Hubei team was able to hold on, but as the Shanghai team's prowess gradually emerged, the Hubei team increasingly lagged behind, losing all fighting spirit and finding it difficult to defend, let alone counterattack. The Shanghai team, having won by a large margin, simply went through the motions, so the situation became lax later on, with nothing exciting to report. Spectators began to leave one after another before the game was even finished.

The First Half Was Quite Competitive 157

The first half was quite competitive. Shanghai's first goal was scored by right winger Tong Rongwen five minutes after the start of the game. The second goal was shot by Wang Yongjie, and the third was a cross from Fu Hexuan, with Tong Rongwen rushing in. The first half ended with a score of three to zero. After switching sides, about three minutes into the game, Chen Jiaqiu scored a goal. After the Shanghai team scored four consecutive goals, Hubei finally opened their account. This goal was scored by Hubei's right inside forward, taking advantage of Shanghai's inside forward's carelessness. The fifth goal was kicked in by Chen Jiaqiu. Tong Yuwen scored the sixth, and the seventh, eighth, and ninth goals were all scored consecutively by Chen Jiaqiu. Among these two goals, the first was thanks to Tong Rongwen's passing, while the latter two were the result of mutual assistance from the three midfielders. The result was a score of nine to one. Referee Yue Xiurong.

The Tianjin basketball team has high hopes for a championship in this tournament. In their first match, they overwhelmed Jiangxi with a score of one hundred and fifty-three to four, creating great momentum. They seemed confident that the basketball championship would be theirs. Yesterday at 1 PM,

they met Jiangsu in the second round. Jiangsu's strength was also quite formidable, as they had defeated the resilient Guangdong with a score of forty to twenty-seven. Their organized formation was evident. After 12 o'clock, the stands around the court were packed, and no fewer than a thousand spectators were standing along the short railings. The lively atmosphere was an unprecedented record for this basketball tournament. ▲Tianjin Takes the Lead First

All paths were blocked, and Jiangsu could not attack, so they passed the ball within their own territory, trying to lure the opponent out to fight, and then seize the opportunity to enter. However, Tianjin remained unmoved, each guarding their defensive positions, without the slightest slack.

Problems Arise in the Women's 200-Meter Relay Race 162

▲East Special District and Guangdong Tie for First Place

▲East Special District Claims to Have Finished First

▲The Tournament Decides to Continue the Race Today

▲The Athletics Championship Rests on This One

Third: Hubei, Fourth: Liaoning Have Already Been Decided

Yesterday at 3 PM, there were six teams in the final of the women's 200-meter relay: East Special District, Guangdong, Hunan, Hubei, Beiping, and Liaoning. The most promising teams were, of course, East Special District and Guangdong. The lineup for East Special District was Liu Jingzhen in the first leg, Wang Yuan in the second leg, Wu Meixian in the third leg, and Sun Guiyun in the anchor leg. The lineup for Guangdong was Situ Wei in the first leg, Huang Shuwei in the second leg, Zheng Li in the third leg, and Liu Youqing in the anchor leg.

The strengths of the two teams can be said to be evenly matched. At the sound of the starting gun, Guangdong took the lead. By the end of the third leg, Guangdong was about two meters ahead of East Special District, and Guangdong was still in first place. After Sun Guiyun's hard chase, she almost caught up with Liu Youqing at the finish line. The referees were unable to distinguish between first and second place, so they decided to rerun the race between East Special District and Guangdong once at 1 PM today to determine first and second place. According to the women's track and field results, other than the 200-meter relay race, Guangdong was in first place with a total of 20 points, and East Special District was in second place with a total of 17 points. The relay race is worth ten points for first place, six points for second place, four points for third place, and two points for fourth place. If East Special District wins first place today, then their total score will be 27 points. If Guangdong wins second place, then their total score will be 26 points, a difference of one point. East Special District will win the women's track and field championship; otherwise, it will be won by Guangdong. Therefore, today's 200-meter relay race is of great importance. It is expected that the two teams will have an extremely fierce competition. The third place has already been determined as Hubei, and the fourth place as Liaoning; there will be no rerun. Representatives from East Special District have lodged complaints with the referees, claiming that East Special District was first and not agreeing to a rerun.

East Special District and Guangdong Tied for First Place in the Women's 200-Meter Relay Race. East Special District Disagreed with the Referee's Decision and Lodged Complaints for a Long Time. After Dai Jitao's Mediation, They Finally Agreed to Continue the Race Today.

Men's Volleyball

Second Round, Group One: Guangdong Wins Over Jiangsu 169

▲A Score of Two to Zero

▲Guangdong Team's Front Line Is Good

At 9 AM on the 5th, Guangdong and Jiangsu met in the second round. The Guangdong team has long been famous and is also qualified for the championship in this tournament. The Jiangsu team's players are all from South China and are skilled in this sport. Their strength is also quite good, but compared with Guangdong, they are still slightly inferior. From observing yesterday's game, the Guangdong team's front two rows of formations were very tight. The attack was very strong, but the back row defense was poor. The Jiangsu team's points were often scored by hitting the back area. At the beginning of the competition, the Guangdong team's momentum was strong and unstoppable. Chen Congchao served and scored eight points in a row, intimidating the Jiangsu team. The subsequent battle was extremely fierce, and the Jiangsu team also gained some points. In the first half, Guangdong took the lead with eleven to two. After switching sides, the Jiangsu team made a concerted effort to counterattack, once gaining a six to twelve situation. Seeing the unfavorable situation, Guangdong quickly cheered up, and the lifts and spikes were very exciting. The spiked balls were often able to hit the mark at will, entering the weak spot. Observing their spiking method, they always waited for the ball to be less than a foot above the net before jumping and hitting hard. Therefore, the ball fell quickly and powerfully, forming a diagonal straight line, making it most difficult for the opponent to defend, which was the key to the Guangdong team's victory. Therefore, they continued to win, winning the first set with twenty-one to twelve. In the continued match, the Guangdong team took advantage of the victory to pursue, intensifying their efforts. Jiangsu became even more unsustainable. Before long, they won again with twenty-one to two, resulting in a score of two to zero. Referee Wu Bangwei. The lineups of the two teams are listed on the left.

Brief History of Athletes 180

Four Ladies from the Eastern Special District

Yesterday's 200m Women's Relay Race, from the Harbin side, are the four ladies Sun Guiyun, Liu Jingzhen, Wang Yuan, and Wu Meixian. Their brief history is described below:

Ms. Sun Guiyun is from Shandong, 16 years old. Ms. Liu Jingzhen is from Jilin, 18 years old. Ms. Wang Yuan is from Wujiang County, Jiangsu, 16 years old. Ms. Wu Meixian is from Yixing County, Jiangsu. The four ladies have been friends since childhood and have a deep relationship. They initially only studied together and occasionally did outdoor sports after class. In 1928, they went to Fengtian to visit the Eastern Provinces Joint Games. Because they felt they lacked experience, they did not dare to participate. However, after seeing the results of the women's track and field events in the venue, there were no particularly special records, so they participated as guests. The results of the competition showed that their performance in each event actually exceeded the previous women's records. They became famous in the three provinces and practiced even harder after returning. They successively joined the Special District Federation and also gained a great reputation. Ms. Sun also won first place in the track and field event and first place in the overall school score. Last year, she also joined the North China Games. With Ms. Sun's efforts, she could have won first place in the overall score, but due to non-compliance with the procedures when registering, ten points were deducted, barely ranking second. She also joined the Sino-Japanese-German Games. Ms. Sun competed with the Japanese athletes, and the Japanese athlete broke the world record with 12 seconds in the 100m. Ms. Sun also won third place with 13.7 seconds, truly opening a new era in the history of women's sports in our country. On weekdays, the ladies engage in sports together, all year round, getting up at dawn to study hard, and never wasting any time after class, which is why they have achieved such results. Ms. Sun is still young and her physical strength is not yet fully developed, but she is already able to do so. If she continues to improve and work hard in the future, she will definitely take the lead in women's track and field in our country. As for Ms. Liu, Wang, and Wu, they are all promising talents and can be said to complement Ms. Sun. May you all strive hard!

Odds and Ends 181

▲ Strive for the Future

The Jiangxi athletes have suffered consecutive defeats in track and field events, lost to Tianjin in basketball, and were defeated by Zhejiang in volleyball. Therefore, the team, with no other records, had already left Hangzhou and returned to Jiangxi yesterday.

▲ Consistency

In the 10,000m race, the last one was Shao Wenlong from Ningbo Fourth Middle School in Zhejiang. After everyone else had finished running, Mr. Shao still had two laps to go. At this time, in the square, thousands of eyes were on him as he ran alone. However, Mr. Shao remained calm and unhurried as he advanced, eventually reaching the finish line. Chairman Dai Jitao said when the 10,000m race was halfway through that if anyone could finish the entire race, even if they were the last one, he would personally award a gift to encourage their consistency.

▲ Women's Misfortune

During men's sports, except for injuries on the field and internal illnesses, there is always the possibility of exercise. However, if female athletes are forced to exercise when their period suddenly arrives, the damage they suffer may be ten times greater than natural illnesses. In this conference, some female athletes from various provinces and cities were unable to participate due to their period, or were forced to exercise due to their circumstances, resulting in most of their results falling behind. This is truly the misfortune of female athletes.

▲ Harming People

After the female short-distance running general Sun Guiyun won first place in the 50m and 100m finals, fellow athletes all congratulated her and asked to treat them. Ms. Sun was also beaming with joy and finally agreed to their request. Yesterday, she treated her guests, which spread quickly. The athletes all knew that anyone who won first place had to treat others, and even those who won second or third place could not avoid it. Therefore, athletes in the venue were constantly asking for treats, and the sound could be heard everywhere. Those who were hit said that Sun Guiyun was harming people.

The Scene of the Start of the 10,000m Race, Photo by Wang Kai 182

▲ Miss Sun Sheds Tears

Yesterday, in the women's 200m relay race, the referee suddenly announced that the first and second places were indistinguishable, and Guangdong and Harbin, etc., had to rerun today. Ms. Sun Guiyun burst into tears upon hearing this, shouting "I'm so angry!" and refusing to race again. It was also said that she did not eat dinner that night. People were quite worried, as the lady had already cried and starved herself. They were afraid that other steps would be taken, and the referee could not bear this great responsibility.

▲ Turpentine Oil's Magical Effect

Harbin athlete Ms. Sun Guiyun has been in the limelight. Readers only know that her results are outstanding, but they do not know where it comes from. It turns out that the first time the lady appeared on the field, Huang Jingwan applied turpentine oil to her legs. As a result, she won first place. She was very grateful to Mr. Huang. From then on, she would always ask Mr. Huang to apply oil as usual, and it never failed. Mr. Huang and others followed her before and after, serving her diligently, and prided themselves on the effectiveness of applying oil to the lady, considering it a supreme honor. In recent years, they have considered this the most enjoyable thing in social situations.

▲ Playing Along

Yesterday at noon, when the second half of the first football match began, a yellow dog suddenly appeared in the Jiangxi camp. It chased the ball and ran left and right, greatly hindering the progress of the players. The sound of applause shook the entire field.

▲ Fence-Sitting Psychology

The venues inside the conference are either connected or separated. Those in separate venues cannot pass through unless they purchase a general ticket and must purchase another ticket. However, those in the highest-level seats in the grandstand of each venue can see from Venue A to Venue B. Clever people often try to get this position as quickly as possible, which can kill two birds with one stone. According to the speculation of those with keen minds, the psychology of such people mostly belongs to those who are fence-sitters.

From September 16th to 20th of the third year of the reign of Emperor Xuantong of the Qing Dynasty, the meeting was held at the Nanyang Industrial Exposition venue in Nanjing and was named the First National School District Team Sports Alliance Meeting, which is now known as the First National Games. The sports categories were divided into track and field, football, tennis, and basketball. Track and field was further divided into advanced group district competitions, secondary group district competitions, and national school joint competitions. The one with the most points was awarded the championship. At that time, there were no restrictions on the participation of athletes. Those who joined the advanced group could also join the secondary group. ▲ Second Session Results

The Second National Games was held on May 21, 1914, at the Temple of Heaven in Beijing, hosted by the Beijing Sports Promotion Association. The competition method divided the country into four parts: East, West, South, and North. The sports categories were divided into six items: track and field, football, baseball, volleyball, basketball, and tennis. The scoring method was as follows: in track and field, except for the five-item and ten-item events where the first place received 5 points, the second place 3 points, and the third place 1 point, each item's first place received 3 points, the second place 2 points, and the third place 1 point. In ball sports, the first place in the four items of football, baseball, volleyball, and basketball received 5 points, and there were no points for the second and third places. In tennis, whether single or double, the first place received 3 points and the second place 2 points. The rankings for track and field were as follows:

▲ Third Session Results

The first two sessions of the conference did not have specific rules regarding various competitions, participating groups, and scoring methods. The Third National Games, held in Wuchang, Hubei in 1924, can be considered the official National Conference. Xiong Bingsan was the chairman, and Zhang Boling was the chief referee. Except for swimming and baseball, which were overseen by Westerners, the rest were managed by Chinese personnel. Participants included the East China, North China, Central China, and South China regions. The Overseas Chinese Youth Association of Little Luzon also sent a basketball team to participate. All sports followed the rules of the Far Eastern Games. The results of the competition were as follows: East China won football, baseball, and tennis doubles; North China won track and field, basketball, and tennis singles; Central China won swimming; and South China won volleyball. Based on the above calculations, East China and North China each won two and a half championships, with the same results. According to the regulations of the Far Eastern Games at the time, when the results were the same, the team that won the track and field overall championship would be the overall champion of the conference. Therefore, in the Third National Congress, North China was first, East China was second, Central China was third, and South China was fourth.

China Science Society 188

Biological Research Institute Enters Sichuan to Collect Specimens

Since its establishment, the Biological Research Institute of the China Science Society has achieved remarkable results. This spring, Director Bing Nongshan specially dispatched a collection team to enter Sichuan on a large scale to collect specimens. The team is divided into animal and plant groups. The plant group is led by Mr. Fang Wenpei, and the animal group is led by Mr. Xu Xifan. Mr. Fang is a graduate of Southeast University with a degree in agriculture and has a lot of research on plant taxonomy. He is also from Sichuan and has been sent by the institute to collect plants in Sichuan twice before, so he is very familiar with the situation in Sichuan. Mr. Xu is a graduate of Xiamen University with a degree in science and has discovered five new species of parasitic roundworms, a new species of jellyfish, and a new subspecies of armored turtle. He has also been sent by the institute to collect in the middle reaches of the Yangtze River and the coastal areas of Fujian twice, so his knowledge and experience are also very suitable. The Ministry of Education highly approves of this move by the society. In addition to issuing passports, it also informed the Sichuan Provincial Government to instruct the troops stationed in various parts of Sichuan Province to provide practical protection for the collection team. It is also heard that all sectors of the military and political circles in Sichuan have always admired the society's undertakings, so this time they will provide financial assistance to the collection team to enable the team to achieve greater results. The Ministry of Health of the National Government, the Institute of Physical Chemistry of the Central Research Institute, the Lin Yuan Committee of the Premier, and the Xiaozhuang Rural Normal School have all made special commissions to the collection team and provided them with financial assistance of 500 yuan each. The Beijing Jingsheng Biological Survey Institute has also specially dispatched two collectors from the institute, Mr. Tang Jin and Wang Fazan, to join the collection work. It is heard that the plant group of the collection team has already entered Sichuan two weeks ago, led by Mr. Fang Wenpei. The animal group only set off yesterday to enter Sichuan because Mr. Xu Xifan had just returned to Beijing from collecting in Fujian.

Free Talk

Laughing it Off 191

— Hai Ke

▲ A Fierce Wife — You say the man goes out at night. Is it really a person or a ghost?

A Henpecked Husband — I'm unlucky to be a person. If I were a ghost, you'd be afraid of me.

▲ Woman A — Oh my, why is your house in such a mess? It seems like you're missing quite a few things. Are you moving soon?

Woman B — No. My daughter is getting married soon. She thinks many things are hers, so she's packing them all up.

▲ Woman — No matter how beautifully you speak, how much you say you love me, I don't want to marry you. The husband I want to marry must be upright and generous.

Man — Then you might as well marry the redwood Eight Immortals table left by my great-grandfather. Nothing could be more upright or more generous.

▲ Company Manager — Can you do shorthand?

Applicant — Yes.

Company Manager — How many words can you record in one minute?

Applicant — I haven't calculated it myself, but every time my wife scolds me, she strings together a whole series of curses like "May you be killed a thousand times, killed ten thousand times, die in the street, die like a dog, die like a ghost," but I can remember it all.

Company Manager — Very good. Your skills are just like mine. Come to work tomorrow.

Detailed Record of the World Tour Group's Arrival in Shanghai 192

— Huang Yingdai

Regarding the news of this world tour group arriving in Shanghai from the United States, although various newspapers have published it briefly, they were not detailed. Now, based on Western newspapers, I record the details to enrich this talk.

The tour group, traveling the world on the German-American Hamburg Company's Resolute ship, arrived in Shanghai at 9 a.m. on April 1st. The number of people was as many as 383. After arriving in Shanghai, they first traveled by car through the International Settlement, and then by rickshaw to tour various parts of the city. After the tour, after 12 p.m., they went to the Astor House Hotel for lunch. That night at 8 p.m., they set sail for Qinhuangdao to tour, etc.

The leader of the group is Captain Cruise, a famous traveler who has traveled around the world as many as ten times. His experience in traveling is self-evident. Since the departure of this tour group, it has passed through as many as thirteen countries, such as Canada, Argentina, Spain, Brazil, Cuba, the Netherlands, Belgium, the United Kingdom, France, Austria, Germany, and Romania, etc., all of which have been visited. The members can represent twenty-nine states and seventy-nine cities and towns in the United States. The number of people is truly rare.

When the tour group was in Shanghai, although the time was limited, when these people were dining at the Astor House Hotel, the hotel specially set up a temporary shop to display various rare items and antiques for the members to choose and purchase. When these people passed through Nanjing Road, the stores were immediately filled with customers and became extremely busy, especially silk and embroidery shops, which were particularly busy, because most of the tour group liked to buy these items.

This tour group departed from New York on January 6th. The majority of the members were Americans, totaling 330. There were 16 Germans, 12 British, 12 Argentinians, 3 Swiss, and one or two each from Austria, Belgium, Brazil, Cuba, Czechoslovakia, Rosenberg, the Netherlands, Romania, and Spain. From now on, they plan to go to Beijing, Seoul, Kobe, Yokohama, Nagasaki, Osaka, Honolulu, San Francisco, Los Angeles, the Panama Canal, and return to New York on May 27th. In addition to the scheduled itinerary, if convenient, they also plan to visit islands, famous people's tombs, and the Himalayas in various places.

Among these 383 people, 224 are male and 159 are female. If we statistically calculate the age of each person, the average is 49 and a half years old. The youngest is Miss Bai Long, who is only seven years old, and the oldest is Mr. Bai Lunga, who is 78 years old this year. The difference between the old and the young is 71 years, and they are also two important roles in the tour group.

Anecdotes from the National Games 193

— Hu Yaguang

When the Games opened, important figures from the National Government were all present, such as Chairman Chiang, Dai Chuanxian, Chu Minyi, and Wu Zhihui, each of whom gave a speech. Chairman Chiang's speech was particularly earnest, repeatedly stating his points in a voice as loud as a bell, until he was exhausted and hoarse. This showed his emphasis on the mission of this conference. The athletes were all moved, and those who had come from afar, such as Liao Ning, also applauded to express their welcome.

Among all the female athletes, they all had short hair and stood up straight. Only one woman from Liaoning had a single braid, which caught everyone's attention and was called a "maverick" of the whole field.

There were vendors in the field selling paper cup ice cream. At this time of chilly spring, if the athletes drink a few cups after being tired, it may easily lead to illness, which seems to be unsanitary. I sincerely hope that the authorities will improve this.

The female athletes are fiercely majestic and do not yield to the men. It is expected that the results will not be bad. In the track and field events, Wang Yuan of Harbin is the most promising, as he has repeatedly won championships in the preliminary selections. Let us wait and see.

The public buses can directly reach the entrance of the venue, and the price is also cheap. However, on the first day, because they were preparing to welcome all the athletes in the auditorium at night, many buses stayed and did not carry passengers. The general public, who were not athletes, were all complaining.

The merchants in Hangzhou, this year, in addition to the incense market, have a large number of tourists. Everyone is happy, saying that this is a good phenomenon after the Party's rule. After the exposition, this is the second grand gathering.

In addition to the male and female athletes showing off their good skills, the busiest in the field are the general photographers. At the sound of the gun, they rush to take pictures of the first and second place winners, and quickly mail them to the Shanghai newspapers. Their enthusiasm and courage are truly admirable.

Phoenixes Fly Together to Western Shores 194

— Meng Yu

Mr. Xu Shiqi from Shexian, Anhui, is a talented and extraordinary young man, an expert in fine arts. His wife, Ms. Yang Manhua, is beautiful and intelligent, with calligraphy and painting skills that match her husband perfectly. They are truly rare talents from our hometown. Mr. Xu recently works in the Ministry of Health of the National Government and has been specially sent by the Ministry as an inspector to Europe, and also serves as a solicitation committee member for the National Exposition Representative Office. He will set sail on April 5th. Mrs. Manhua has aspirations for a grand tour and will accompany him to see the sea. In the future, when they return, they will surely add weight to the motherland. The twin phoenixes in the clouds will fly to the West. All friends are competing to give them a farewell feast.

▲ Against the Wind. On March 27th, maritime celebrities such as Ge Gongzhen hosted a public banquet for Mr. Xu at the Dahua Hotel, celebrating his mission to a foreign country and his wife's accompanying him to study fine arts. They knew that I was not a casual friend of Mr. Xu, so they sent invitations to share the grand occasion. However, I had to go to Hangzhou for business and returned to Shanghai that afternoon at 4 p.m., unable to join the feast. Although I will invite Liang Meng to Jinlong Restaurant tomorrow to make amends, the crime of arriving late is unforgivable.

▲ Sincere Gifts. Mr. Xu, feeling that he will be leaving the country soon and will not return for more than a year, invited ten close friends, both male and female, to a dinner party at his residence on Xin Zha Road on the 31st. The food and wine were certainly abundant, but Mei Qu believed that the guests were all the best of their time, and the two hosts were sincere and refined, like a first draft of the Huangting Sutra, just right, the flavor was truly beyond the food and wine. Mr. Xu and his wife had a collection of collaborative calligraphy and painting, which they had solemnly presented to me the day before. The sincerity of the gifts was at its peak.

▲ Why Envy Immortals. This was what Mei Qu said to me after the gathering on the 31st. Mei Qu had only met Mr. Xu once, more than three years ago. This time, Mr. Xu solicited paintings to prepare for participation in the exposition, and unexpectedly obtained a portrait of a lady by Ms. Mei Qu's son, Yunhua. Mr. Xu said, "She was my top student when I taught at the Meizhuan in the past. At that time, she only studied Western painting, but now she studies national quintessence. Such rapid progress is admirable. Therefore, I also admired Mei Qu's literary talent and asked me to send her a local invitation to the meeting that day. Mei Qu admired the elegant and peerless couple, their art and talent surpassing the crowd. She said to me, "Can you not write a poem for the two beauties, Xu and Yang, based on the line 'I only envy mandarin ducks, not immortals'?"

The Comedy of Yushan Also Being Called Niushan 195

— Zhou Chu

I once traveled to Yushan in Changshu with a friend. Someone asked me, "Have you ever heard that Yushan is also called Niushan?" I said, "Mencius said that the trees on Niushan were once beautiful. That mountain in the state of Qi must be in today's Shandong Province. I have never heard of Yushan in Changshu having that name." Someone else said, "It exists. Yushan is named after Zhong, while Niushan refers to its shape. Niutou (cow's head) refers to Ziyou's tomb. Niujiao (cow's horns) refers to Xinfeng Pagoda. Niuhou (cow's rear) refers to the Laoshi Cave. There is also a Niuwei (cow's tail) that was broken off by Qin Shi Huang's whip. The relics still exist today. The cow is so huge that it refers to the entire city of Changshu as a barrel for feeding the cow." These words are extremely humorous, and Changshu scholars can all say them." I heard these words and dared not believe them. Later, I saw a Yushan Ballad by Mr. Hu Shiyu of Kunshan, which was a travel poem, printed in oil and shown to friends. Yushan Ballad is one of them. Reading it can verify the above. The poem says, "Although Yushan is small, its name is known throughout the world. I have never heard of replacing Yu with Niu. Now I ride a bamboo sedan chair around the mountain, and the chair carriers chatter and bother me. Their words are strange and baseless, let us just say it and just listen to it. They say that this mountain is named Niu after its shape. Niutou refers to Ziyou's high tomb. The entire city carries it as a barrel for feeding the cow. Xinfeng Pagoda stands tall like two horns. Niuhou expels arrows at Laoshi Cave. The tail below is suddenly broken off and should feel pain. In the past, the Qin Emperor Shi Huang drove the cow to Xihu (West Lake), but the cow would not rise. (Shanghu is also called West Lake) He raised his whip and roared with a thousand pounds of force, striking down and breaking off its tail. Its tail is slightly distant and forms a small hill, which is now submerged in the wilderness. Why not go and see it to prove my words? It is only a mile or two ahead. The words of the rustic men of Qi are wonderful. I also casually spoke and almost lost my laughter. The wind on the seven waters of Qinchuan is cold, and I face the cow and play ancient tunes."

Casual Talks in the Capital 196

— Lu Shuwen

Over the years, driven by hunger, I have wandered aimlessly, drifting like tumbleweeds, and struggling in hardship. Recently, I left Hangzhou and entered the capital, where I plan to stay for a while. What I have seen and heard has given me mixed feelings. I am writing this with a pen, and the article starts and ends by itself. I am not making a fuss about nothing, nor am I seeking to develop a great work. I write when I am inspired, and I do not continue at a fixed time. I do not dare to be different, but I want to preserve the truth. I am writing casual talks.

Those who talk about the lack of repair in the capital's municipal administration often attribute it to the incompetence of the authorities. If we discuss it fairly, with such a large and dilapidated urban area and the current financial constraints of the city treasury, it is not easy to talk about construction. Let alone wanting to imitate London and New York in an instant. However, without a definite plan, no事业(shi4 ye4) can be achieved. The chaotic and unsorted state of the capital's urban area cannot be reformed and improved in a short period of time. If we can assess the situation and establish a long-term plan for a hundred years, and with the efforts of the authorities and the assistance of the people, we can improve things in order of urgency, then after a few years, there will be a significant change. And the key to the grand plan should be to decide on the road system first. Otherwise, if orders are changed in the morning and evening, and decisions are uncertain, the people will doubt and hesitate and dare not invest. Even if the authorities can make efforts, what will it help the development of the city? The road system in the capital has been planned several times and has only recently been decided. It was officially announced the day before yesterday. From now on, there will be a path to follow and hope for construction. The investors of the people will also have a guarantee of safety. Is this not beautiful? I deeply hope that after the authorities have made a decision, they will be able to abide by it permanently and not make any more changes. Then New York and London will have a day to emerge in the East. I feel that the announcement of the trunk road system by the Capital Construction Committee is a great event for the capital, and I record it as such.

Among the famous scenic spots in the capital, the ones in the city are not as good as the suburbs. In the city, places like Mochou and Qinhuai are either ruined and dilapidated or have become noisy markets. Jiming and Beiji are also ugly due to poor decoration. Those that are worth climbing and glancing at are all outside Stone City. The depth of Qixia Mountain, the seclusion of Yanziji, the majesty of Zhongfu, and the simplicity of Houhu (i.e., Xuanwu Lake) are the most famous. Others, such as Niushou Mountain, Yuhua Terrace, Longtan, and Shizishan, are all worth seeing and can be used for sightseeing. However, apart from these, there are still places that are extremely secluded, particularly charming, and have not been noticed by people, such as Xinglin outside Taipingmen. The place is located at the foot of Zijin Mountain, three miles away from Taipingmen. There is a vast expanse of flat land, with apricot flowers lining the road, interspersed and meandering. Following the slope into the mountain, near the third month of spring, the jade-like apricot flowers are in full bloom, covering the mountain and creating a magnificent view. At the end of the apricot flowers, it is right at the陰(yin1) of Zhongfu. The deep valleys and high mountains are inaccessible to birds. Walking with Laiyi, scooping up泉水(quan2 shui3) and drinking it, whistling and wandering in it, all worldly worries are cleared away. I went there with Wu Zicheng and sighed at the beauty.

▲ Correspondence. In the "Free Talk" published on April 3rd, there was a section called "Female Chicken Turning Male," signed Fei Gongzhi. Is this the same Xiang who was in Hangzhou and tested養氣(yang3 qi4) with Dahe at Zhang Gongci and gave me a silk painting of a lady? I have not seen him for thirty years and miss him very much. Warmth in My Heart (164) 197

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 10: Blazing Flames Reaching the Sky, A Filial Daughter on the Balcony; Red Carpet on the Ground, Meeting Famous Actors on the Spot

In that play "Worse Than Going Home," the most important person playing the leading role of the prodigal wife is... didn't they say that in their Qingliu Society, there are two people who are good at playing young ladies, one is Jiang Xiaoxia and the other is Ou Yuqing? But Jiang Xiaoxia is still in Japan at the moment and has not returned to China. He is studying fine arts and aspires to go to France. France is the source of European fine arts. He wants to prepare for their fine arts academy, so even just looking at it with his eyes will increase his knowledge a lot. But Ou Yuqing went back to his hometown after returning to China. It turned out that he was from Liuyang County, Hunan. During the Reform Movement of 1898, Liuyang produced two martyrs, one was Tan Liuyang and the other was Tang Liuyang. Talented people were born in the land, and the small Liuyang became famous. Ou Yuqing's father was also an official. He was also from a scholarly family. After returning to China, he had to return to his hometown to visit his relatives once, so he was not in Shanghai either. But in this play "Worse Than Going Home," there was already a specific person playing the prodigal son. This person's surname is Ma, and his style name is Jiangyou. When it comes to looks and acting, Ma Jiangyou is not as good as Jiang Xiaoxia and Ou Yuqing. But he has a special feature, because he is good at acting in tragedies. And the heroine of "Worse Than Going Home," the prodigal wife, has a very deep lung disease. Ma Jiangyou also has a very deep lung disease. One side of his face naturally carries a pale and bloodless look. He doesn't even need makeup. He naturally has a face of tuberculosis. Therefore, he is most suitable to play the heroine in this play. Only his voice is not very sharp and has a bit of a crying tone. It is very unsuitable in other plays, but it is not a big obstacle in this tragedy. He performed it once when he was studying drama in Tokyo and received a lot of praise. They have now arrived in Shanghai, so they chose to perform this play "Worse Than Going Home" because Jiang Xiaoxia and Ou Yuqing are not in Shanghai. Only Ma Jiangyou is here, so they chose this play. Secondly, they discussed the issue of location. At that time, the voice of so-called reformed drama in Shanghai was loud. They called those vernacular dramas without gongs, drums, or strings "civilized dramas," also known as "civilized new dramas." Adding the word "civilized" above shows that the old dramas were not very civilized. But from the perspective of people with a little knowledge, the so-called civilized dramas are also limited in civilization. No matter who it is, without any practice, they jump onto the stage and shout and jump around randomly. People who understand a little bit of the superficialities give a speech to the audience, as if they are teaching people in general. The rest is incoherent and he doesn't even understand the plot. He doesn't even know what's going on. There are such theaters in Shanghai. There are also all kinds of scenery, and there are even rotating stages. They often use "Large Rotating Stage" to publish large-character advertisements to promote a group of ladies to come and see.
