Reasons for the Stagnant Sale of Foreign Funds 202

This year, the inflow and outflow of foreign funds from other ports has been extremely quiet, far less prosperous than in previous years. The main reason for this is mostly due to the impact of the current situation and the obstruction of transportation. In the northern route, due to military relations, commerce has invisibly stagnated, and there is naturally no need for purchases. Even if there are outgoing shipments, they are nothing more than military supplies. In the southern port, due to sluggish exchange and consumption, the use of foreign funds has also felt delayed. What is currently being shipped is purely British dollars and two types of new coins, just to embellish the market scene and to supply the demand for Hong Kong dollars in the relaying ports. In past years, the Hankou port should have been in the peak season for all kinds of goods, and the use of funds would have been most frequent. Unexpectedly, it is now in the scope of war, so it cannot be launched. Therefore, the current source and demand are minimal. Yesterday, only over 200,000 arrived from the Yangtze River, 300,000 were shipped from the northern route, 300,000 were shipped from Hankou, 200,000 new coins were still shipped from the Guangdong gang, 30,000 British dollars, and 150,000 spot dollars were shipped to the interior, prepared as rice funds.

Oil Market: White Tung Oil from Hankou Drops Continuously 205

The rise and fall of white tung oil depend on whether there are transactions from foreign firms. This has been the custom for nearly ten years and has not changed slightly. This time, however, it slightly deviates from the norm. Half a month ago, the transaction volume of foreign firms was originally not large, and domestic sales also stopped due to the end of spring sales. The market was silent and there was no possibility of development. However, it suddenly rose sharply like a dragon from the sky. The reason is that although there was continuous rain this spring, the spring water upstream of the Yangtze River did not rise, resulting in a gradual decrease in the source in Hankou. Therefore, a slight transaction can easily trigger a price increase, and the lack of inventory everywhere can also lead to an increase. At that time, domestic sales were slightly prepared for inventory everywhere, and the business in Hankou saw the situation of rising prices due to the thin inventory. The transaction of foreign firms was handled up to 26 taels and 7 qian according to foreign regulations, but only dozens or hundreds of tons. Domestic sales in Hankou also sold up to 21 taels and 6 qian according to foreign regulations. After this increase, the prices in Zhejiang also increased to 34 yuan and 8 jiao and 35 yuan per dan for river delivery. However, the increase was not at the right time, it was just a flash in the pan. In the recent three or four days, a telegraph from Hankou came, saying that tung oil had arrived, and the market immediately turned flat and weak. Yesterday, the telegraph reported that a foreign firm sold 500 tons of May futures oil for 25 taels, 7 qian, 5 fen and 7 qian, which had already fallen by about 1 tael. According to the arrival of more goods, it is also expected that it will fall again. If the mountain in Shandong collapses, the bell in Luoyang will respond, and it is feared that it will be difficult for Zhejiang oil to maintain its price.

Change of Name of the Tea Trade Association 210

▲Changed to Shanghai Foreign Firm Tea Trade Association

The trade association in this port was originally the only group of foreign firms' tea business internally and externally. Since the National Army established its capital in Nanjing, various industry groups have gradually corrected themselves. In order to comply with the regulations for the correction of commercial groups promulgated by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, the association has decided to change its name to the Shanghai Foreign Firm Tea Trade Association from this month.

Mr. Tian Tong was originally invited to lecture on "Today's Food Problem," but Mr. Tian suddenly fell ill and could not attend the meeting, so Mr. Chen Hansheng, director of the Social Group of the Academia Sinica, was invited to lecture on What is the Chinese Land Problem. ▲Second Election of the Yinnan Yu Clan Shanghai Association: The Yinnan Yu Clan Shanghai Association Declares: The Yu Clan in Shuangxi, Yin County, is a famous clan, and the Yu Clan is considered the most among the Yin people who live in Shanghai. The association has a glorious history and outstanding achievements in the past, which is praised by the Yin people. In this election, everyone is pleased to have found the right people.

The publisher is the Asia Fine Arts Book and Newspaper Compilation Office, 33 Liyaxiya Street, Huayuan Street, Jiangwan Road.

Medical News

▲Xie Liheng is Good at Treating Measles: Last winter was very cold, and now spring is still chilly. The toxins of coal smoke and fire stoves are breathed into the body and are difficult to expel, so there are many measles in children, which are both serious and dangerous. Dr. Xie Liheng from Ningli, North Zhejiang Road, is famous for his good treatment of measles. Whenever he encounters a dangerous case, he often comes up with a unique method to turn danger into safety. For example, the granddaughters of the world-renowned Ren Yixu Xiaoxu, Weng Yousan, an employee of the Zhabei Water and Electricity Plant, and Liu Baisheng, the captain of the Sanbei Company, all recovered completely from dangerous and severe measles.

News of Female Students of China Public School 215

Ms. Hu Suying and Ms. Wang Huali: Anyone who has seen the 25th anniversary parade of China Public School will surely notice a pair of roles performing a double act. One is a lively, cute, and interesting Fengyang woman, played by Ms. Hu Suying, and the other is a dull and earthy Fengyang old man, played by Ms. Wang Huali. Ms. Hu has never participated in any school activities. Somehow, she actually performed on stage at the parade that day. Her lively figure, her skillful performance, her fluent lines, her clear throat, and her interesting makeup, even her every move, every word, and every smile, all aroused the audience's cheers. When she performed to the right place, the entire audience held their breath and there was no sound, like the quiet atmosphere of the believers in the church listening to the pastor's etiquette report, which also showed the amazing art of Ms. Hu. The Fengyang old man played by Ms. Wang was crude and stupid. From her makeup of the figure-eight beard and her dull and rude expression, we cannot see that she contains the slightest identity of a daughter. Her humorous wit, her wonderful dialogue, and Ms. Hu just made an excellent foil. The two ladies have indeed made considerable achievements in the study of art.

The Establishment of the Women's Basketball Team: Since the China Public School basketball team participated in the Jiangnan Six University standard competition, it won the battle against Jiaotong University and then won the battle against Chizhi University. Therefore, the China Public School basketball team, which was known for its awkwardness, began to be noticed by the general public in society. Recently, the school authorities, feeling the silence of the female students' sports, organized a female basketball team this semester. A few days ago, the newly organized China Public School female basketball team held its first establishment meeting in the school's gymnasium. Lei Yueqin was elected as the team leader, and Li Hanyanwen was elected as the clerk. From then on, whenever the evening sun sets and the evening breeze is cool, we often see a group of female generals wearing red and green, flying skirts and dancing sleeves, performing their best skills on the female basketball court. How strong is their interest! (Jiang Ping)

The Mock Court of Great Xia University 216

Universities with law departments should naturally have mock court practices as part of their curriculum; it's not some particularly novel or unique initiative. However, although our university, Great Xia, has had a law department for several years, this is our first attempt at mock court practice. This semester, after hiring Mr. Jiang Zhensan to teach a practical course in civil procedure, he used his extensive experience to diligently prepare for the court session and ultimately achieved his goal. It is said that the audience was particularly enthusiastic when the mock court opened on that day, and all parties were fully prepared, engaging in eloquent debates, creating a grand scene. Those who were present even forgot that it was a mock court, and the excellent results in the future are certainly to be looked forward to. Regrettably, the author was unable to personally attend the grand event due to other matters on that day, and still feels regretful when thinking about it.

The case heard by the mock court on that day was determined in advance by the professor in charge. It involved three brothers, Zhang Yi, Zhang Bing, and Zhang Jia. Zhang Yi was adopted into another family as a child. Later, Zhang Yi had no son, and before his death, he established Zhang Jia's only son, Zhang Geng, as his heir. The inherited fertile land of three thousand acres, a residence, and a city property were all inherited and managed by Zhang Geng. Zhang Bing's eldest son, Zhang Wu, claimed that Zhang Geng's inheritance as the only son to continue the lineage was illegal, as he had three brothers and should inherit Zhang Yi's lineage. The inheritance should also belong to him, so he filed a lawsuit in court. Zhang Geng also argued that his inheritance was based on the fact that he was of the same lineage and could inherit multiple ancestral temples, and that Zhang Wu had borrowed one of the city properties left by Zhang Yi and should return it to him. All parties presented their cases to the court, and the question was how to judge the case.

In addition, the characters in the court on that day and those who played the roles were also assigned in advance by the professor in charge from among the students. The list is recorded below: Judge Wu Linkun, Judges Chen Xinghua and Yan Hanqing, Clerk Tu Kunfan, Prosecutor Yang Huilong, Court Officers Ban Guihua and Lu Jingyuan, Plaintiff Lawyers Wen Dairong and Liu Zhiquan, Defendant Lawyers Wang Shuxun and Shen Ergu, Plaintiff Li Yanpan, Defendant Qiu Zhendong, Interested Parties Zhang Jia, Qian Langxi, Zhang Yi Zheng Tigan, Witnesses, Witnesses in the Plaintiff's Inheritance Document, Zhou Zhengli, Lin Mingzhong, Zhu Dihua (Zhi Jing)

Theater News 217

Golden Theater Premieres "Buddha's Enlightenment" - The Golden Grand Theater announced that the film "Buddha's Enlightenment" depicts the compassionate deeds of Buddha Shakyamuni's life on the one hand, and denounces the extravagance and licentiousness of the Sadohan Royal Palace in India on the other. It is truly a good remedy for the prevailing frivolity, indulgence, and shamelessness of recent times. The Golden Theater has been premiering this film for several days, perhaps also out of concern for the declining state of the world's morality, it is said. ▲ Wei Lie Film Company Goes to Hangzhou to Shoot News - Wei Lie Film Company announced that its manager, Mr. Hong Weilie, led a team of assistants to Hangzhou a few days ago to shoot news footage of the National Games. They will return to Shanghai for processing in about a week, so that it can be supplied to various cinemas for screening, it is said. ▲ "The Three Great Heroes" Has Been Filmed - Xifan Film Company announced that its twelfth production, "The Three Great Heroes," is directed by Mr. Hu Zongli and stars the up-and-coming female martial arts star Wang Feijuan. The play is a martial arts romance drama, and Wang's martial arts and performance are remarkably impressive. The play features flying swords and scientific electric light battles, and the filming techniques are quite novel and unexpected. The interior and exterior scenes of the play have been filmed, and the company is now rushing to produce subtitles and editing, and will be ready for a preview screening soon, it is said.

▲ South Palace Drama Society Established - The South Palace Drama Society announced that it held its founding ceremony yesterday at the Baixing Xilai Society. Sixty members attended, a mix of men and women, making for a very lively occasion. The entertainment segment in the program added a lot of color, especially Ms. Xin Ruiying's lullaby, which was sung with a beautiful voice, like a new oriole emerging from the valley. Mr. Pan Shiju's "Cinnabar Mole" had accurate articulation and clear pronunciation. Mr. Yang Deyong's portrayal of a beggar was also excellent, imitating the "Mao Mao" tune with humorous lyrics, making the audience laugh. By the time the meeting ended, the city was ablaze with lights. The committee members of the society have been selected as Mai Mengxia, Mao Bixin, Xiao Jianqing, Pan Shiju, and Yu Fengzhi, it is said.

▲ Flying Girl Song and Dance Troupe to Hold Inaugural Performance - The Flying Girl Song and Dance Troupe announced that it was organized by Mr. Wang Junwuqi and will hold its inaugural performance on April 17th, 18th, 19th, and 20th at the Guanghua Grand Theater at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Avenue Messena. The troupe will also perform new songs, including "Her Heartless Serenade," it is said.
